Disarmament Conference Fails, Great Powers Compete to Expand Armaments; Swanson Seeks to Realize World's Leading Naval Power by Striving to Build New Warships Within Treaty Limits 42

Seattle – After U.S. Secretary of the Navy Claude Swanson inspected the naval base at Pearl Harbor in Honolulu, he returned here today. He told people that if his plan succeeds, the U.S. Navy will not lag behind others in the world. According to Washington sources, Swanson's plan for naval construction is likely to be fulfilled. Before Germany withdrew from the Disarmament Conference, many in U.S. military circles believed that after the Disarmament Conference reached a disarmament agreement, it would be possible to open the way for major powers to significantly reduce their navies in 1936. Now, even those close to the U.S. President say that regardless of whether Geneva can reach an agreement this year or next, the U.S.'s original naval plan is unlikely to change.

Some naval officers have heard that Britain may suggest changing the naval construction plan to limit the maximum displacement of cruisers for each country to 7,000 tons. Given the tense situation in Europe, it is expected that both Britain and the U.S. will maintain the provisions of the existing London Naval Treaty. After Swanson read the reports from Washington and Geneva here, he did not comment, but reiterated his claim that a strong navy is the best guarantee of peace. Swanson did not indicate whether he had any suggestions for improving the naval base in Honolulu. However, it was learned from other sources that Swanson seemed to pay more attention to the need to improve some buildings than to fortifications. Swanson also said that the main purpose of his trip was to understand the true nature and current status of the naval facilities in each base, and whether they needed repair and improvement. The Secretary of the Navy must know these things in detail in order to request funds from Congress or approve or reject the requests of naval officers. Swanson will now inspect the Bremerton Naval Shipyard near here, and then visit the Mare Island Naval Shipyard and San Diego near San Francisco. (Guomin News Agency dispatch, 17th)

(London) The Labor Party's newspaper, the "Daily Herald," reported that the British Admiralty not only demanded that it engage in shipbuilding within the scope of the naval treaty, but also planned to replace old ships. The Admiralty expects that the naval treaty will expire on December 30, 1936, and that there will be no possibility of extension. It plans to build 25 new cruisers and several ocean-going warships of 25,000 tons equipped with 12-inch guns. In addition, it also requires the construction of 15 torpedo boats per year to replace 100,000 tons of old ships, and 10,000 tons of submarines. The newspaper also said that the number of naval personnel will also increase by 10,000, and that the Air Force Department also plans to request the construction of a large number of aircraft. (Havas dispatch, 18th)

Warlike Nations Refurbish Naval Array, Standing Fleet Reorganized in October, Recruiting Elite to Fully Demonstrate Power 43

▲Tokyo News. The Standing Fleet for the Japanese Navy's ninth fiscal year is scheduled to be implemented on the 15th of next month (November). This newly formed fleet has a new and invincible array, recruiting the elite of the navy. The Japanese authorities attach great importance to the reorganization of this fleet in preparation for emergencies. Among the main forces of the fleet, the giant ships Mutsu, Kongo, and Hyuga, which were active in the eighth fiscal year, will first be withdrawn from the front line in anticipation of the dangerous period of 1935 and 1936. They will be replaced by the Ise, Kirishima, and Fuso, all of which have been remodeled to have great power and a new look. The 7th Squadron will be replaced by the Nagara and Isuzu, replacing the Abukuma and Yura of this year. The 33rd Destroyer Squadron, led by Yubari in the 1st Torpedo Squadron, will take a rest in the name of reserve ships. The light cruiser Sendai (5,195 tons), which has been dormant for a year, will serve as the flagship, enriching the surprise attack force. The 22nd Destroyer Squadron will be replaced by the 29th Destroyer Squadron. The 1st Submarine Squadron will once again be heavily burdened by the mother ship Jingei. The 2nd-class cruiser Yura will be moved from the 7th Squadron and incorporated into the flagship. As for the 1st Air Squadron, which holds air supremacy, the 26,900-ton Akagi and the new small aircraft carrier Ryujo will be included in the fleet, replacing the Kaga and Hosho. The 4th Squadron of the 2nd Fleet, the 10,000-ton ships Chokai, Maya, Atago, and Takao will continue to exert their power. The Aoba, Kinugasa, and Kako of the 6th Squadron, which was resurrected last year, will continue to participate for two years. The Jingei will serve as the 2nd Submarine Squadron. In short, this newly formed combined fleet recruits the elite of the Japanese Navy and is sufficient to fully demonstrate the power of the invincible fleet. The most noteworthy feature is the allocation of a submarine squadron, which distinguishes the flagship from the mother ship. The details are listed below.

First Fleet 44

1st Squadron: Haruna, Ise, Kirishima, Fuso; 7th Squadron: Nagara, Natori, Isuzu; 1st Torpedo Squadron: Sendai, 5th Destroyer Squadron: Asakaze, Harukaze, Matsukaze, Hatakaze; 23rd Destroyer Squadron: Mikazuki, Kikuzuki, Mochizuki, Yuzuki; 29th Destroyer Squadron: Yufukaze, Oikaze, Hayate; 30th Destroyer Squadron: Udzuki, Minadzuki, Mutsuki, Yayoi; 1st Submarine Squadron: Flagship Yura, Mothership Jingei; 28th Submarine Unit: Submarine I-59, I-60, I-63; 30th Submarine Unit: Submarine I-65, I-66, I-67; 2nd Torpedo Squadron: Jintsu, 7th Destroyer Squadron: Ushio, Oboro, Akebono; 8th Destroyer Squadron: Asagiri, Yugiri, Amagiri, Sagiri; 11th Destroyer Squadron: Shirayuki, Fubuki, Hatsuyuki; 12th Destroyer Squadron: Murakumo, Shirakumo, Usugumo; 2nd Submarine Squadron: Mothership Jingei; 1st Air Squadron: Akagi, Ryujo; 2nd Destroyer Squadron: Minekaze, Sawakaze, Okikaze, Yakaze;

Second Fleet 45

4th Squadron: Chokai, Maya, Atago, Takao; 6th Squadron: Aoba, Kinugasa, Kako; 18th Submarine Unit: Submarine I-55, I-53, I-54; 19th Submarine Unit: Submarine I-58, I-57, I-56; Sasebo Naval Base Guard Ship Tatsuta; 26th Destroyer Squadron: Kuri, Kaki, Ume, Yomu; Mako Naval Base Guard Ship Kuma; 4th Destroyer Squadron: Hayakaze, Akikaze, Tachikaze, Hokaze; Maizuru Naval Base Guard Ship Tama; (World News Agency)

European Countries Seek Path to Peace 46

(Geneva) The Disarmament Conference has been temporarily postponed, and from Geneva to various European capitals, efforts are now being made to find a way to world peace through disarmament. National representatives are rushing back to their countries to plan how to deal with the emergency situation caused by Germany's actions. U.S. Representative Davis has stated that the United States is only concerned with world disarmament and does not want to be involved in political events. It is widely believed that unless Germany rejoins the talks, disarmament is unlikely to be achieved. (Reuters dispatch, 17th)

France Expresses Policy of Maintaining Cooperation but Unwilling to Abandon Interests; Daladier Explains Budget Proposal; Current Government Position Solid 47

(Paris) France's first official reaction to Germany's withdrawal from the Disarmament Conference was officially announced today by French Prime Minister Daladier in the National Assembly's House of Representatives. France is prepared to continue to cooperate for peace but is also unwilling to abandon its rights. Subsequently, after the National Assembly listened to the government's budget report, it responded to the government's request for immediate consideration of the budget with a vote of confidence of 470 to 120. It is widely believed that this move by the National Assembly can be regarded as full support for the policy announced by the Prime Minister. Daladier did not use any radical language towards Germany, only stating that France is neither deaf to words nor blind to actions. He believes that negotiations should continue and asks rhetorically, "If you want to reconcile, why break up first? If you are willing to accept complete disarmament, why can't you accept a plan that guarantees effective disarmament?" He then declared that France is not isolated and that there are more allies today than since the World War. He also said that France is in a position to protect its territory and independence. He then discussed Germany's withdrawal from the Disarmament Conference and the League of Nations, saying that this shows that a new element is still needed in the organization of the peace structure. France has already studied this element and continued, "We are prepared to follow a policy of international cooperation regardless. The reasonable attitude we have already expressed and the sacrifices we have made are enough to allow us to maintain this policy. However, our willingness to continue this international cooperation does not mean that we are willing to give up our rights." Finally, he said that France will attend the Disarmament Conference, which will reopen on October 26, in order to follow this policy. After Daladier finished his speech, he submitted the budget proposal. (Guomin News Agency dispatch, 17th)

(Paris) Today, the House of Representatives approved the government's financial proposal to make up for the budget deficit with 470 votes to 220 votes, making an emergency debate. Although the government proposes to make up for the shortage by increasing taxes and reducing government spending, there are many difficulties. The right wing is prepared to support reducing government spending, but not increasing taxes, while the left wing is the opposite. The government's emergency plan includes special sales tax, gasoline tax, civil servant pension tax, and reform of certain monopolies. In addition, there are also gasoline import tax and military equipment monopoly. The government also hopes to raise 650 million francs through national lotteries. It is difficult to predict whether the government's proposal will pass. If the Daladier government falls, a national mixed cabinet will probably be formed. (Reuters dispatch, 17th)

Important British Cabinet Meeting: Holding a Wait-and-See Attitude Towards the European Situation 48

(London) The cabinet meeting convened at 11:00 AM. According to British custom, the cabinet holds regular meetings every Wednesday. In addition, the cabinet will also decide on Britain's future attitude in Geneva. (Havas dispatch, 18th)

British Foreign Secretary Refutes German Accusations: Accommodation of Germany Has Been Documented; Reasons for Withdrawal Unacceptable 49

(London) British Foreign Secretary Simon issued a statement today, saying that Britain announced last December that Germany should enjoy equal rights in terms of security. Britain still adheres to this declaration today. However, serious events have already occurred. Although our promises will not be changed, the details of fulfilling this promise must be slightly different. Recent events have made people increasingly fearful. This is the real reason why countries with substantial military preparations hesitate and worry and are unwilling to weaken their armed forces hastily. As a result of our worries, Britain is now more worried about the international situation than it has been for many years, and the European continent is even more worried than Britain. Simon then elaborated on the steps taken in Geneva to accommodate Germany's demands, saying that a compromise was almost reached last week. I then asked Germany what it meant by "sample" weapons. Surprisingly, Germany did not explain the meaning of "sample" but insisted on substantial rearmament. Now, German Foreign Minister Neurath accuses me of distorting the facts. This statement is completely wrong. I can publish various documents and records. Our hard work in good-faith talks, even if not destroyed by Germany's final attitude, has been hindered. He completely cannot accept the reasons given by Germany for its withdrawal. Baldwin once said that any country that makes disarmament impossible will have no friends in the world. This is very true. Britain does not want to cause ill feelings and is willing to find ways to promote good cooperation between countries and to do its utmost to find an honorable way to solve the great problem of humanity's hopes for the future of the world. (Reuters dispatch, 17th)

(London) After British Foreign Secretary Simon arrived here by plane from Paris today, he immediately went to the Prime Minister's residence to consult with Prime Minister MacDonald and Lord President of the Council Baldwin for an hour. Simon told reporters that German Foreign Minister Neurath stated that the German side had informed the British Foreign Secretary of Germany's views on October 6, but the British Foreign Secretary did not accurately convey these views. He said that he would sincerely regret it if there were discrepancies between him and the German Foreign Minister on the incident. However, the British people can rest assured that the so-called inaccuracies do not belong to the British side. It was found that the German Charge d'Affaires in Britain sent a letter to the British Foreign Secretary on October 6, informing him of Germany's views on disarmament. Germany simultaneously sent the same official document to the Italian government but did not send it to the French and American governments participating in the talks. Because the British Foreign Secretary believed that Germany's opinions were of great importance to the disarmament issue, after research, he immediately recorded a copy and sent it to the French and American ambassadors stationed in London. (Reuters dispatch, 17th)

"Peace and Equality": Germany Truly Seeks It Day and Night; Hitler Convenes Party Meeting to Promote the Election Campaign 50

(Berlin) The leaders of the National Socialist Party and its military convened a meeting. Prime Minister Hitler personally delivered a speech, saying, "Our struggle for equality of rights has now entered the final stage. This struggle is inextricably linked to the German nation's struggle for economic recovery and for daily bread. The pacification of world politics is an indispensable condition for curing chronic economic diseases. Previous German governments believed that it would be beneficial to participate in international conferences before we obtained equality of rights. This was a big mistake, because they were poisoned by 'Geneva' and therefore were pessimistic about Germany itself and optimistic about the League of Nations. I am not. I am quite optimistic about our country and pessimistic about Geneva and the League of Nations. It is precisely because Germany has left the gloomy atmosphere of Geneva that Germany's love of peace is now even greater than before. The German government responds to all humiliating demands with the following sentence: 'We want peace, but we do not want others to treat us, Germany, as a second-class country.' This answer is endorsed by the entire German people. The National Socialist Party has been fighting for rights in Germany for fourteen years. Today, Germany must also maintain its rights in diplomacy with the same determination and perseverance, maintain the demand for equality of rights, honor, and loyalty, which are by no means empty and impractical. Germany wants peace and seeks nothing but peace. In the future, Germany will never sign any alliances and treaties that do not treat Germany equally. There is a limit to leading the people; beyond this limit, it is not justified. Our election propaganda is extremely important, because this election will be a moral test and a struggle for national rights related to life and death. The National Socialist Party members' love of peace is probably greater than anyone else in Germany, because National Socialism is theoretically based on bloodline laws and racial concepts and is an internal movement. Therefore, any imperialist policy of external aggression is despised. However, when necessary, we can also have the determination to protect our due rights, which is the same as our rejection of violent policies. Our party's election campaign should focus on this serious issue, and any secondary issues may be temporarily put aside. In the coming weeks, the German nation will be filled with a deep and sacred sense of seriousness. The passionate emotions of the Germans are not merely emotions expressed on the surface but are based on a deep belief in due rights. The German nation can have this attitude entirely because of its belief in the leader, because these leaders know the importance of their responsibilities and duties and will do their best to fulfill them." Hitler then elaborated on the necessity of the future election, saying that it would be sufficient to prove the freedom of National Socialism. "The National Socialist Party has begun the great task of re-assisting within the German nation, and it must be completed in the future. This struggle is for the benefit of the entire country. Therefore, even our domestic enemies, we are willing to carry on friendly terms with them, but only on one condition: that they must voluntarily promote the honor of the German nation and love peace." Finally, he called on the National Socialist Party to abide by discipline internally. (Havas dispatch, 18th)

Change of Commander of the French Far East Navy 61

(Paris) Vice Admiral Taigude was appointed yesterday as the French Navy Commander in the Far East, replacing Vice Admiral Pédrel, whose term has expired. Taigude was born on May 2, 1879. He entered the naval academy at the age of eighteen and was sent to China in 1900 (i.e., the Gengzi Year). He came to China for the second time in 1910. During the European War, Taigude commanded torpedo boats in the Aegean Sea and made repeated achievements in battle. After the armistice, he served as commander in the Atlantic and Mediterranean fleets and held important positions in the Naval General Staff. From 1927 to 1928, he was appointed Director of General Affairs of the Ministry of the Navy. In 1928, he was promoted to Vice Admiral and is currently the Chief of Staff of the Toulon Fortress. (Havas dispatch, 18th)

At 5:00 PM today, the main force of the revolutionary army retreated from Bangkok to Korat. It is expected that Siam will not be threatened again for the time being. Eighteen government planes flew over Chachoengsao, dropping several bombs as a warning, and sent a ship to open fire several times. The large revolutionary army in the area immediately surrendered. As a result, the railway south of Bangkok has been restored, and it is expected that it will return to normal within a few days. The revolutionary army near Siam gradually began to withdraw last night. The Korat Airfield was evacuated first and reoccupied by government forces. Initially, it was expected that the revolutionary army would pretend to retreat to lure the government army out of the city to ambush them. However, the situation today seems to indicate that the revolutionary army has lost its momentum. Seven government planes have crashed in three days. The seventh one crashed on the roof of the government's palace on Monday morning. (National Telegram, 18th)

Regulations for Distribution of Personnel Who Passed the Higher Examination 68

(Nanjing) The National Government issued an order on the 17th to promulgate the Regulations for the Distribution of Personnel Who Passed the Higher Examination. This order:

Regulations for the Distribution of Personnel Who Passed the Higher Examination

Article 1: These Regulations are formulated in accordance with Article 9 of the Civil Service Appointment Law and Article 18 of the Implementing Regulations of the Appointment Law.

Article 2: The distribution of personnel who passed the Higher Examination shall be handled in accordance with these Regulations.

Article 3: Personnel who passed the Higher Examination shall report to the Ministry of Personnel within the registration period announced by the Ministry of Personnel in accordance with the following provisions, but may do so in writing: (1) Filling out a preference form; (2) Submitting two recent 2.5-inch half-length photos; (3) Submitting the examination certificate and experience documents.

Article 4: After the registration deadline, the Ministry of Personnel shall prepare a list of the registered personnel, according to their ranking in the examination category, and the proposed distribution agencies and personnel quotas, and submit it to the Examination Yuan for submission to the National Government for distribution to the relevant central or local agencies.

Article 5: When the Ministry of Personnel considers the preferences of the personnel who passed the Higher Examination for distribution, it shall proceed in accordance with the following standards: (1) If there are too many personnel requesting distribution to the same preference, those who rank higher in the Higher Examination shall be given priority for distribution. The remaining personnel shall be distributed according to their second preference. (2) If there are too many personnel requesting distribution to the second preference, those who rank higher shall still be given priority for distribution. (3) If there are still quotas remaining after the distribution of the previous two items, the distribution shall be decided by the Ministry of Personnel. The provisions of the preceding paragraph shall not apply to current or former civil servants of the relevant agencies who have passed the examination and request to be distributed to the original agency for service.

Article 6: Personnel who passed the Higher Examination shall be assigned to various agencies for appointment, except as otherwise provided by laws and regulations, if they have served in the Commissioned Rank for more than two years and submit accurate documentary evidence of their appointment and removal dates, which is verified by the Ministry of Personnel. Those who have no prior experience or whose prior experience is less than two years shall be assigned to various agencies for study.

Article 7: If there are no corresponding personnel vacancies in the agencies to which personnel are assigned for appointment, they may first be appointed to the Commissioned Rank and paid a salary of one-half or more of the initial level of the Recommended Rank.

Article 8: Personnel assigned to various agencies for study shall be assigned duties by the assigned agencies and assigned relevant personnel to be responsible for guidance. During the study period, they shall be paid a salary of one-third or more of the initial level of the Recommended Rank.

Article 9: If the original salary of current personnel who are initially assigned or assigned to the original agency for appointment or study is higher than that specified in these Regulations, they shall be paid according to their original salary.

Article 10: The study period for personnel assigned for study shall be one year. Those whose performance is rated A after the study period shall be assigned by the Ministry of Personnel for probationary appointment as Recommended Rank officials. Those whose performance is rated B shall have their monthly salary reduced by 10% and their study period extended by half a year. Those whose performance is rated C shall have their monthly salary reduced by 20% and their study period extended by one year. However, the extension shall be limited to two times. Those whose performance is still rated below A after the expiration of the period shall have their study and appointment suspended.

Article 11: If the assigned agency considers the performance of the personnel assigned for study to be excellent during the study period, it may appropriately shorten their study period and request that the Ministry of Personnel assign them to the relevant agency for appointment in advance.

Article 12: The performance of the personnel assigned for study during the study period shall be filled in the study performance evaluation form by the assigned agency, together with the study diary, and submitted to the Ministry of Personnel for review and decision.

Article 13: When personnel who passed the Higher Examination in different categories are assigned to the same agency for appointment, they shall be listed separately according to their examination categories. When vacancies occur, the head of the agency shall supplement them separately in accordance with the provisions of Article 5 of the Appointment Law.

Article 14: If the assigned agency cannot appoint or study all of the assigned or assigned personnel, it may distribute them to its subordinate agencies separately in accordance with the standards specified in Article 5, but the distribution situation must be reported to the Ministry of Personnel for record.

Article 15: If any of the following circumstances apply to the assigned personnel, the Ministry of Personnel may request the Examination Yuan to submit a request to the National Government to change the assignment or transfer the assignment: (1) When the Ministry of Personnel deems it necessary; (2) When the central or local agencies transfer personnel; (3) When the assigned personnel submit a request due to special circumstances and it is approved by the Ministry of Personnel, but each person is limited to one time. Those who already have positions may not do so until they have been appointed for one year.

Article 16: Personnel assigned for appointment shall report to the assigned agency within the time limit prescribed in the schedule after receiving the assignment credentials. Personnel assigned for study shall report to the assigned agency within the time limit prescribed in the schedule after receiving the assignment study document. The deadline for arrival shall be calculated from the day following the receipt of the credentials or documents. Those who cannot arrive within the time limit shall state the reasons in detail and submit them to the assigned agency for review and approval.

Article 17: Personnel who passed the Higher Examination who do not comply with the provisions of Article 3 shall not be assigned or assigned. Personnel assigned for appointment or assigned for study who do not comply with the provisions of Article 16 shall have their appointment or study suspended.

Article 18 The format of the preference form, study performance evaluation form, study diary, distribution schedule, and assignment credentials shall be determined by the Ministry of Personnel.

Article 19 These Regulations shall be implemented from the date of promulgation. (Central News Agency dispatch, 17th)

Communist Bandits Launch a Surprise Attack on Pingxiang; He Jian Reports on the Relief of Pingxiang; The Two Communist Forces of Xiao and Cai Have Both Collapsed 76

A dispatch from Changsha states that the communist bandits Xiao Ke and Cai Huiwen led the false 17th and 18th Divisions, numbering over 10,000 men and carrying 5,000 to 6,000 guns, and on the 13th

Advanced on Pingxiang and Liling in three routes. The people of the provincial capital were greatly disturbed. He Jian, the Commander-in-Chief of the Western Route Army, was on the 9th, returned to the province from Pingxiang via Xiangdong to participate in the National Day commemoration. He was originally scheduled to return to Pingxiang by special train at 8 a.m. on the 13th to convene a meeting of the Western Route Army generals to discuss the suppression of the bandits, but due to the bandit Xiao's attack, he suspended his departure and remained in Changsha. At 9 a.m. today (the 16th), various party, government, and military circles held an enlarged memorial week in Zhongshan Hall. He Jian personally attended and reported on the recent situation of bandit suppression in the Pingli area, saying that the siege of Pingxiang has been lifted, and the Western Route Army launched a pursuit on the 16th before dawn.

An excerpt from his report is as follows: "I (He referring to himself) originally scheduled to leave the province on the morning of the 13th on an inspection tour, but on the evening of the 12th, I received a report that the two bandits Xiao Ke and Cai Huiwen led all the bandits out of Yongxin, attacking Pingli in three routes. The central route, with about three to four thousand men, attacked Pingxiang from Daluli; the right wing, with about three to four thousand men, attacked Pingxiang from Lugongbei; and the left wing, with about two to three thousand men, attacked Liling from Meitianqiao. At that time, our army in Pingxiang only had one regiment of Liu Jianwen, and Meitianqiao only had two companies of security regiment soldiers stationed in bunkers. The military strength was vastly different, and the situation was tense. That night, I urgently dispatched the two regiments of He Shisheng and Ouyang Xin to rush to the aid of Liling Meitianqiao on the morning of the 13th. At the same time, I rushed to compile three detachments to rush to the aid of Pingxiang overnight. The 62nd Division Commander Tao Guang's troops were compiled into one detachment, gathering in Pingnan to fight nearby; the 19th Division Commander Li Jue's troops were compiled into one detachment, departing from Changsha by special train to Liling on the morning of the 13th, then transferring to Pingxiang; and the 63rd Division Chen Guangzhong's troops and the 16th Division Commander Peng Weiren's troops were combined into one detachment, rushing to the aid of Pingxiang from Lianhua. On the morning of the 14th, the Xiao bandits occupied Mashan, twenty li away from Pingxiang. The front line had already reached Qibao and Shanwan, six li away from the city. Pingxiang was besieged. Fortunately, Commander Tao arrived and engaged the bandits fiercely near Mashan, resulting in many casualties on both sides for several hours. Fortunately, two airplanes arrived and bombed, killing many bandits. The bandits could not hold out, and Commander Tao occupied Mashan. The bandits who had advanced to Qibao and Shanwan turned back and besieged Commander Tao, engaging in a fierce battle for several hours, even resorting to hand-to-hand combat. Commander Li Jue arrived from Changsha and made contact with Commander Tao, launching a joint attack. The bandits could not hold out, and on the 15th at Shenshi (3-5 PM), the entire line wavered and began to retreat. Pingxiang was turned from danger to safety, and the city siege was lifted. Because it was late that day, we stopped advancing. Now, our three detachments have all concentrated in Pingxiang, and we are scheduled to track down and pursue them in different directions before dawn today (the 16th). It is said that the Xiao bandits are now fleeing back to their old nest in Yongxin. As for the force that attacked Meitianqiao, they had only a slight contact at 1 PM on the 13th. Seeing that our reinforcements had arrived, they retreated to Dongqiao without any fierce battle. Another small force destroyed the railway and telegraph lines at Laotao on the 13th, but did not stay and also went to Dongqiao. All the damaged lines were restored on the 14th. According to the captured bandits, the Xiao and Cai bandits were ordered by the false central government to unite with the Kong bandits and He Chong to attack Pingli, so as to cut off the Western Route Army's communication with the national army in Jiangxi and seize the base of the Western Route

Army (the headquarters of the Western Route is located in Pingxiang) and destroy the defenses on the west bank of the Gan River. Fortunately, I was still in Changsha and Chief of Staff Liu Yinggushang remained in Pingxiang, so the mobilization of the troops was very fast, otherwise the damage would have been great," and so on. Finally, he also urged the people of various counties in Hunan Province to rush to repair bunkers and consolidate the rear to prevent the westward escape of the Gan bandits. After the speech, the crowd dispersed. Now that the people know that the bandits have fled, the market is very safe. He Jian originally planned to go to Jiangxi to meet with Chiang that day to discuss something, but fearing that the people would be suspicious, he decided to sit in Changsha for the time being and not start his journey. Once the Xiao bandits and others are completely defeated, he will still make a trip to Jiangxi. (October 16th)

Fang Ji Leaves the Army; Military Affairs in Northern Hebei End; Fang Ji's Negotiations with Shang Zhen Are Successfully Completed; Shang Zhen Sends Troops to Escort Him to Tianjin 77

A dispatch from Beiping states that Fang Zhenwu and Ji Hongchang's troops plotted to attack Northern Hebei for over a month. Some days ago, they sent personnel to Beiping to negotiate surrender. However, it is reported that yesterday (the 16th) at 4 PM, Fang Ji had already left the army and went to Tianjin, preparing to go abroad. His troops will be inspected by the authorities, and then dispersed and reorganized. The details of the situation are as follows:

Fang Ji's actions this time were to unite with the troops of Tang Yulin, Liu Guitang, and Wang Ying. At the beginning of occupying Da and Xiao Tangshan, their momentum was extremely strong. Later, due to the strict blockade by Wan Fulin's troops and others, it was not easy to advance. In addition, supplies of provisions and ammunition could not be delivered, so a meeting was held. It was decided that Tang Yulin and Wang Ying's troops would return to Chahar, while Fang Ji would lead his troops east to retreat. They then arrived in the area of ​​East and West Dulin Village, where they were

Prevented by the Japanese army from advancing further. He had no choice but to send Wang Zhongfu and others to Beiping again the day before yesterday to negotiate surrender, requesting guarantees for his personal safety, cessation of oppression, and reorganization of his troops. The Beiping authorities stated that everything would be no problem, but Fang Ji and others must leave the army first. However, a response was required by 12 noon on the 15th. Wang and others immediately telegraphed Fang Ji. Fang Ji replied in a telegram that he could leave the army first, requesting the Beiping authorities to send a Eurasian Aviation plane to pick him up, or for Beiping's diplomatic and charitable organizations to send personnel to escort him to the front, or to allow him to bring a small number of guards to Shunyi to facilitate his disguise and departure. The Beiping authorities did not grant Fang Ji's request and again limited him to formally expressing his attitude by 10 a.m. yesterday (the 16th). At the same time, they additionally sent Guan Linzheng's troops to the Yang Yiying and Fengjiaying Kuliushu areas to prepare for an ambush. Yesterday morning at 9 a.m., Xu Tingyao, Guan Linzheng, and others went to the front to deploy. At around 10 o'clock, Fang Ji again sent Mi Wenhe, the army commander of Fang's troops, Wang Changzhou, the chief of staff, and Hu Xi, the secretary-general, to Fengjiaying to meet with Li Xingcun, the division commander of Shang Zhen's troops, representing Fang Ji, expressing Fang Ji's decision to leave the army immediately, but requesting the following: (1) Guarantee the safety of Fang Ji's life after leaving the army; (2) Fang Ji's troops hope that the Beiping authorities will grant them reorganization; (3) The personnel and a part of the guards who followed Fang Ji hope to be properly arranged or given

Severance pay. They also said that before leaving the army, Fang Ji intended to meet with Commander Shang (Zhen), because Fang and Shang Zhen had a very deep friendship. Li replied that Commander Shang would arrive at the front soon, and all the details could be discussed with Shang in person and there would be no problem. Soon, Li sent Councilor Feng Heming and Staff Officer Jiang Xibin to accompany Mi Wenhe by car to meet Fang Ji. At around 11 a.m., Shang Zhen arrived at Fengjiaying and exchanged views with Xu Tingyao, Guan Linzheng, and others on Fang Ji's aftermath. At 2:30 p.m.,

Fang Ji and Mi Wenhe, etc., also arrived by car with a small number of guards. Shang Zhen went out to greet them and immediately discussed everything at the division headquarters of Li Xingcun. Fang Ji stated that he would leave the army that day to go abroad for investigation, but hoped that the Beiping authorities would properly handle his troops. Then Shang Xu used the telephone to ask He Yingqin for instructions. He granted all of Fang Ji's requests. Fang and others then had lunch at the division headquarters. After everything was settled, Fang immediately ordered his troops to await reorganization by Commander Shang and sent Mi Wenhe to be responsible for the ending. After receiving the order, Mi immediately returned to the defense area and gathered the troops in Dongzhuang, Luogezhuang, Qianhoushaluo, Matouzhuang, Donggezhuang, etc., to await inspection. At around 4 p.m., Fang Ji took the 32nd Army's car and went to Tianjin via Sunhe and Tongzhou. Shang sent a platoon of guards to escort him. Fang Ji arrived in Tianjin that night and stayed at Ji Hongchang's private residence in the French Concession. His actions were extremely secretive. However, according to a certain source, Mr. Fang had not yet arrived in Tianjin and had gone elsewhere midway. What exactly happened will be clear in the coming days.

After Fang Ji left, Shang Xu and others discussed Fang Ji's troops' aftermath and

Front-line deployment. At around 10 o'clock, Shang Xu returned to Beiping in the same car and went to Jurenhall to meet He to discuss the disposal of Fang Ji's troops and decided on several items: (1) Fang Ji's troops will be inspected first, and each soldier will

Be given five yuan and officers will be given yuan, and they will be dispersed and reorganized separately; (2) Guns and horses will be inspected and handed over separately; (3) After the inspection, they will be transferred to Baoding for training and reorganization empty-handed. The meeting dispersed at around 12 o'clock. He immediately issued a circular telegram reporting the resolution situation. The original text of the telegram said, "Fang Zhenwu and Ji Hongchang rebelled and caused harm to the local area. This time, they repeatedly disturbed the vicinity of the Beiping suburbs. After being tightly blocked by the national army, their power was exhausted and they could not succeed. Today, they expressed their surrender to our front-line troops. Fang Ji and others have left the team and gone elsewhere. The remaining remnants are being disposed of. I would like to inform you that I have signed and sealed it, He Yingqin." As for Fang Ji and others, they also issued a circular telegram, stating their anti-Japanese experience and the difficulties of leaving the army this time, as well as their future intentions. The text is more than 500 characters long.

Today, the Military Branch has sent personnel to meet with Zhou Shangzhen's representative Li Jingrong to go to Fang Ji's defense area to inspect the troops. Fang Ji's troops originally had more than 14,000 people. After several battles and the bombing by Japanese aircraft this time, the number of remaining people is still unclear. Now the war in Northern Hebei is over, and the front-line troops will be demobilized immediately. The Japanese army also sent a staff officer to our army's defense area today, expressing that Fang Ji has left and the Japanese army will withdraw immediately. (October 17th)

Zhang Qun Returns to Hankou from Xunyang: He Jian Sees Chiang and Wang in Nanchang and Lushan, Reporting on All Political Situations in Hubei Province 78

A dispatch from Hankou states that Provincial Chairman Zhang Qun, after receiving a telegram from Chairman Chiang calling him to Gan on the 9th, arrived in Nanchang on the 10th, saw Chiang on the 11th, followed Chiang to Lushan on the 13th, descended the mountain to Xunyang on the 16th, and transferred to the Dehe steamboat westward, arriving in Hankou on the 17th. Chiang agreed that after Vice Minister Chen (Yi) returns from leave, Vice Minister Cao (Haosen) will be ordered to return to his post. During this period, it will still be difficult to resign. Regarding the provincial government

Reform issues, I previously received a telegram from Chairman Chiang ordering the provincial government's expenses to be reduced by half to increase county government expenses. I also suggested to Chiang that the various departments of the provincial government should work together and simultaneously seek county government reforms. Chiang has telegraphed eight provincial governments to solicit opinions. I intend that the reform of the provincial system should be decided first, and the reform of the county government is especially necessary, because the provincial government is a design and supervisory agency, while the actual implementation is entirely in the hands of the county government. Wang and Chiang's meeting in Lushan discussed political reforms, but there was no meeting form. The eight-province food conference has been scheduled to be held in Gan. The provincial government intends to submit a proposal and hand it over to Director Jia (Shiyi) to attend. The food relief issue is the key to the rise and fall of the countryside, and it is also the life and death of the farmers. If we do not plan now, it will be too late. A month ago, I, along with Hunan Provincial Chairman He, Henan Provincial Chairman Liu, Anhui Provincial Chairman Liu, and Jiangxi Provincial Chairman Xiong, jointly telegraphed the central government to levy import tariffs on foreign rice to save the industry in crisis. The central government adopted it. Recently, I visited President Wang in Lushan, and he also paid great attention to this. It will be implemented in the shortest possible time. Now it is just a matter of procedure and must be passed by the Legislative Yuan. I also asked for instructions in Gan regarding the political facilities in the bandit area. The most important thing is to implement special education. The required expenses will be jointly raised by the headquarters and the provincial government. The headquarters will bear 40% and the provincial government will bear 60%. With funding, promotion will be easy. The construction of highways is also of great importance. It has now been decided to find a way to complete the seven-province highway plan. In the eastern Hubei area, the existing plan will still be followed to build it. In western Hubei, the original old road in Shihe will be widened and improved." (October 17th)

Zhang Cui Zhenhua's Lawsuit: Yi Peiji Files a Counterclaim, Accusing Cui and Zheng of Conspiring to Sell Out the Appeal to Various Levels of Agencies 79

"For the matter of submitting a petition, I, Yi Peiji, have investigated the case of the Palace Museum by the Prosecutor of the Supreme Court Procuratorate, Zheng Lie, and the Prosecutor, Zhu Shusheng. Zheng Lie's telegram to Zhu Shusheng stated that 'Zhang instructed Yin to come immediately and prepare the fees first,' etc. Yin is the only witness for the public sale of fur goods. It is obvious that the accuser is bribing the witness to help others, committing a crime under Article 180 of the Criminal Law. Subsequently, the Palace Museum clerks Dong Lin and Zhang Zhejilian reported that Yin Qiweng personally stated that Zhang Cui Zhenhua and the Chief Prosecutor Zheng Lie and Prosecutor Zhu Shusheng jointly colluded with the witness Yin Qiweng in all aspects, and the situation is even more obvious. Yi Peiji also found two telegrams from Zheng Lie to Zhu Shusheng at the Nanjing Wireless Telegraph Bureau. One said: 'It can be handled by the local procuratorate and the investigation of the superiors should be expedited... Xiaoyun Geng (Zheng's name is Xiaoyun),' and the other said: 'There is no resistance in this case, Li's criminal suspicion is serious and he should be arrested immediately... Xiaoyun Jia.' Zheng Lie, Zhu Shusheng, and others are derelict in their duties and incite false testimony and false accusations, and the evidence is conclusive. According to Article 180 of the Criminal Law, 'Anyone who intends to have another person receive criminal or disciplinary punishment by falsely accusing the competent civil servant shall be sentenced to imprisonment for not more than seven years. Anyone who intends to have another person receive criminal or disciplinary punishment and forges or alters evidence, or uses forged or altered evidence, shall be punished in the same way.' According to the above sections and the report that Li Zongdong personally wrote a note to purchase fur goods, etc., it has been found that it is indeed forged. Yin Qiweng Zhang Cui Zhenhua committed a crime under this article, and Zheng Lie Zhu Shusheng is the instigator of the second item of this article. Article 123 of the same law states, 'A civil servant who has the duty to prosecute crimes and commits one of the acts listed in each item shall be sentenced to imprisonment for not less than one year and not more than seven years.' Also, the second item states, 'Anyone who knows that a person is innocent but causes him to be prosecuted and punished, or knowingly that a person is guilty but does not cause him to be prosecuted and punished without reason,' Article 139 of the same law states, 'A civil servant who entices a subordinate civil servant to commit a crime under Articles 228 and 139 shall have the original penalty for the crime of enticement reduced by one-half.' Article 140 of the same law states, 'A civil servant who takes advantage of his position or opportunity or method to intentionally commit crimes other than those in this chapter shall have the original penalty increased by one-third.' According to the above sections and Zheng Lie's telegram to Zhu Shusheng, 'It can be handled by the local procuratorate and the investigation of the superiors should be expedited,' etc., and the Jia telegram said, 'There is no resistance in this case, Li's criminal suspicion is serious and he should be arrested immediately.' Zheng Lie Zhu Shusheng has committed the crimes listed above in the Criminal Law. Zheng Lie, as the Chief Prosecutor of the Supreme Court, openly colluded with the accuser, ordering subordinates to buy witnesses and harm innocent people. Such a shocking thing is still rare. I now plan to file a complaint with the Procuratorate of the Jiangning Local Court, but Zheng and Zhu are both the heads of the procurators, and the Procuratorate of the Local Court may not be able to legally detain them. I hereby attach three copies of photos and documents, and petition your Department to promptly dismiss Zheng Lie and Zhu Shusheng and hand them over to the Jiangning Court for investigation and trial to show great fairness and uphold the law and discipline. It is for the public's convenience. I respectfully present this to the President of the Executive Yuan and the Minister of Judicial Administration, Yi Peiji." (End)

According to the above photo, one of the three documents, there are still two types of documents, which are reduced in size for printing, and I am omitting them because I am afraid they will be blurry.

Fujianese Oppose the Levy of Foreign Rice Tax – Because the Province's Rice Production is Insufficient 80

A dispatch from Fuzhou states that the provincial government has decided to abolish the tea export tax and levy a foreign rice import tax, which is now being actively implemented. The Finance Department has appointed Zhuang Taoru as the director of the Provincial Foreign Rice Import Tax Bureau and Wu Lutai as the director of the Southern Fujian Branch Bureau. The head office is located in Fuzhou, and the branch office is located in Xiamen, and they are ordered to open immediately. However, Xiamen rice merchants strongly oppose this. Yesterday, they specifically telegraphed the provincial government, requesting to suspend the implementation. The telegram stated that in a corner of Southern Fujian, except for Longxi and Haicheng

The two counties have slightly rice production, and the bulk of the supply depends on the ports of Yangon and Siam. At a time when bandit disasters are frequent and droughts are disastrous, spring plowing cannot be done and autumn harvest is hopeless. We rely entirely on foreign rice to help us. If heavy taxes are levied again, it will not only increase the burden on the people, but if foreign rice stops being transported, it will inevitably lead to famine. I beg the government to consider the situation and observe the difficulties of the people, and postpone the implementation to comply with public opinion, etc.

According to people in the rice industry in Fuzhou, the provincial capital needs to consume two thousand dan of rice every day, and one thousand dan are transported upstream. The source is two thousand dan transported from Shanghai and Hong Kong every day (of which Chinese rice and foreign rice each account for half), and one thousand dan are transported from the nearby Lianjiang and Changle counties. The price of rice in the market depends on the quantity of sources from Hong Kong and Shanghai and the high and low of the original price. Currently, top-quality rice is about eight yuan and eight jiao per dan, and inferior rice is worth about seven yuan per dan. However, in addition to the two thousand dan imported from Hong Kong and Shanghai, rice used to be transported to the province from upstream every year. This year, not only is there no rice transported to the province from upstream, but one thousand dan must be transported from the province every day. Between the coming and going, there is a difference of three thousand dan every day. With an average of eight yuan per dan, farmers upstream could earn 16,000 yuan a day in previous years. Now they have to spend 8,000 yuan, plus the constant trampling by red bandits over the years, how can the countryside not go bankrupt? Therefore, if the government does not have a fundamental plan to quell the disaster and revitalize the agricultural community, merely levying foreign rice tax is to make the impoverished farmers bear an additional burden of 1,000 yuan every day. But the provincial government has already appointed people to set up bureaus to handle it, so it will be difficult to stop the process. (October 13th)

Shantou National Salvation Association: The Reason for Being Destroyed; Lin Songsheng's Integrated Factory for Selling Taiwanese Wine Was Suddenly Inspected 81

A dispatch from Shantou states that the Shantou National Salvation Association was destroyed by Taiwanese some days ago, as previously reported. The reason for this matter is that there is a person named Lin Songsheng from Chenghai who originally brewed wine with local rice in Tiangang Township, Chenghai. Tiangang is located near the Qiupu coast, where ships come and go, which is very convenient. It is more than ten miles by water from Shantou City and is under the jurisdiction of Xiapeng District, Chenghai. In recent years, Chaozhou local rice has become expensive, and the cost of brewing wine is too high. Lin's ingenious idea was to mix Dutch alcohol from the Netherlands with sugar water to become Shuanghua wine, which was sold on the market and made a lot of profit. Those who didn't know thought it was local wine. After the September 18th Incident, the Japanese yen plummeted, and the alcohol produced in Taiwan was extremely cheap. Lin then partnered with a Taiwanese from Hongfa Foreign Firm on Chaoan Street, Shantou City, to run Taiwanese alcohol. The goods were disguised in the style of iron barrels from Dutch alcohol from Sambulong, Taiwan, and used old-fashioned motor fishing boats to go directly to the coast of the Fujian-Guangdong border, and then used small boats to smuggle them to Tiangang. The integrated winery run by Lin turned Taiwanese wine into counterfeit local wine and then sold it. The factory is a foreign-style house with a cellar underneath. The cellar can hold thousands of barrels of alcohol, each barrel holding 500 gallons. In order to prevent patriotic actions by the public, Lin specially placed two local cannons, fourteen rifles, several short guns, and more than ten fierce dogs to guard the factory site. All wine merchants know about these facts and hate them. Because Lin operates alcohol, the Shantou Aojia Cask Sales Office and the Xiapeng Wine Tax Bureau are all shareholders, helping the smooth growth of his business. Although the National Salvation Association has heard about it, it did not dare to arrest Lin due to too many concerns. On September 30, inspectors from the National Salvation Association went directly to Tiangang Township to search and found 1,105 barrels of Taiwanese alcohol, worth more than 100,000, and decided to transport all the alcohol to Shantou and detain Chen Xuwen and others. However, Lin Songsheng was not arrested. The National Salvation Association knew that the Japanese consulate would definitely interfere, so they checked the evidence that Lin was not of Japanese nationality and decisively charged Lin with the crime of being a traitor.

And offered a reward of 500 to arrest him, and decided to confiscate Lin's property. But Lin seemed to have nothing to fear and was still lying high in the Hongfa Foreign Firm, and told people that he had his own way. Before long, the Japanese consulate made a very strong protest to the municipal government, citing the Sino-Japanese Treaty of Commerce and Navigation, claiming that Chen Xuwen was a worker of Japanese nationals and asking the municipal government to protect Japanese merchants' use of people and not to block the decks of Japanese ships (because boats and boats were not allowed to approach Japanese ships arriving in Shantou). The municipal government forwarded the original letter to the municipal party department of the National Salvation Association for reply. This was the fuse of this case.

At 2 p.m. on the 7th of this month, inspectors Yuan Qiang, Zhang Cheng, and Qiu Fu from the National Salvation Association seized a small boat in the river of the Huilan Bridge, loaded with eight packages of fish fins, and detained the owner of the goods, Chen Shaoyou, and two boatmen to the National Salvation Association for imprisonment. The fish fins were stored in the warehouse. After a while, a clerk from the Lianfa Store on Tongjin Street suddenly came to the association with two Japanese, demanding to hand over Chen Shaoyou and the fish fins. The duty member Ma Zonghan refused. The two Japanese left disappointed. At about 4 p.m., more than 20 armed Taiwanese suddenly swarmed into the National Salvation Association, carrying short guns and holding iron tools, destroying the equipment in the association, scolding and jumping. Then they pried open the warehouse, took out the fish fins, opened the prison door, and released seven people, including Chen Shaoyou, Huang Yashi, Lin Xing, Li Tiequan, Lin Yuchun, Lin Yazhong, and Chen Xuwen, and left swaggeringly. Afterwards, Mayor Zhai Zongxin, Social Section Chief Liang Shunan, and the secretary of the Japanese consulate all went to investigate. Zhai Liang and the National Salvation Association's executive Xu Dingguang went to the Japanese consulate to lodge a verbal protest. It is said that the Japanese consulate strongly denied that there was any instigation or connivance. This is the course of this case. It is rumored that the Japanese consuls in South China have recently decided at a meeting in a certain place to interfere with our people's patriotic movement, so this incident in Shantou may be its beginning, which is also unknown. (October 10th)

Wuxi: Judgment in the Fake Champagne Ticket Case 85

Lu Junyi, the owner of the Fu Ji branch of the newspaper in Qingguoxiang, was selling fake lottery tickets. A young woman, Lu Huifen, purchased a Qingdao Universal Sports Association champagne ticket from the branch, which turned out to be a counterfeit. Because the lottery date was postponed, she sent a letter to the Qingdao office to inquire. The office then entrusted the Shanghai general manager of the Minhua Bank to send someone to Wuxi to report to the First Branch and bring Lu Junyi to court. Afterwards, his younger brother, Lu Junqing, went to Shanghai to lure the broker Shi Xingrong (i.e., Shi Arong) to Wuxi, where he was arrested and brought to justice, and detained together. After the Procuratorate concluded its investigation, it filed a public prosecution with the same-level criminal court in accordance with Article 226, Paragraph 2 of the Criminal Code. Yesterday, Judge Lai Sihug提签 brought the three defendants to court and announced the judgment: Lu Junyi, Lu Junqing, and Shi Xingrong, intending to use them for the purpose of exercising, collected forged and altered valuable securities, each sentenced to three years of imprisonment and a fine of five hundred yuan. After the sentence was pronounced, they were taken back into custody. However, Lu and others declared in court that they would not accept the judgment and would appeal to the High Court.

Zhenjiang: Brief Biography of the New Security Director 87

Yesterday, the Jiangsu Provincial Government meeting decided to appoint Xiang Zhizhuang as the acting director of the Security Department. Here is a brief biography of him: He is currently forty years old, a graduate of the second term of the Baoding Military Academy. He served as a staff member of the Management Section of the Hubei Military Affairs Office in the Xinhai Year. In the first year of the Republic of China, he served as a platoon leader of the Third Battalion of the Ninth Infantry Regiment of the 23rd Division of the Shanghai Army. In the fifth year of the Republic of China, he served as a training officer of the Independent Regiment of the Fifth Division of the National Protection Army in Liangguang, a major staff officer of the Division Headquarters, and concurrently the commander of the Independent Artillery Company. In the sixteenth year of the Republic of China, he served as a lieutenant colonel staff officer of the Headquarters of the 26th Army of the National Revolutionary Army, promoted to major general staff officer. In the 21st year of the Republic of China, he served as the brigade commander of the First Independent Artillery Brigade and was transferred to the education director of the Army Artillery School. In July of this year, he was transferred to the training chief supervision department as a major general counselor.

Yangzhou: Bandit Leader Zhang Zhaoquan Arrested 88

Li Dianzhen, in the third district of this county, was the victim of the Zhang Jingxuan family kidnapping case. Although the ransom has been paid, the bandit leader has not yet been captured. According to intelligence, the bandit leader Zhang Zhaoquan and his accomplices, Liu Si and others, are now hiding in Zhenjiang, using their service in a certain agency as a shield. The county specially dispatched Police Captain Zhu Daixin and detectives Gao Guisen and Jin Chao, together with public security personnel, to Zhenjiang with documents. At 9:00 a.m. on the 16th, they, together with the Zhenjiang detectives, arrested accomplices Xu Fengting and Liu Shifeng in the Chunjianglou. They confessed that they had two boats, moored under the Shifu Bridge. They were found upon investigation, along with three bandit women and four boys and girls. They were immediately transferred to the Fuyun Company's Shunfeng wheel and towed to Yangzhou. The bandits were detained at the Zhenjiang Detective Office awaiting transfer to Yangzhou. Zhang Zhaoquan (formerly known as Zhou Erzi) was also detected in the crowd and was transferred to Yangzhou on the Zhenjiang-Yangzhou train in the afternoon. The team leader Zhu Hui and detective Gao Guisen preliminarily interrogated him that night. It was reported that Zhang Zhaoquan had confessed to the kidnapping of Zhang and Jingxuan's two children and that a gun was stored at the home of a certain family in the Taizhou area. Xu, however, denied joining the bandits. The county government is currently being consulted for further investigation.

Large Quantity of Opium Seized

Gong Guoliang, the fifth district chief of the Jiangsu Provincial Water Police, received a report that a large quantity of opium was transported from Yichang and unloaded at Sanjiangkou, Zhouzhou, in recent days. He specially dispatched special squad leader Yin Xiu to lurk in the reeds on the Jialu patrol ship. On the morning of the 16th, around 4:00 a.m., they saw the Ewo's barge arriving at Sanjiangkou, throwing several paper bags into the river and sounding its steam whistle before leaving. Soon, two small boats came to retrieve them. Knowing that they were transporting opium, they immediately fired shots to stop them. The oil bags were seized, containing dozens of catties of opium, and seven opium peddlers were arrested, including three young men in Western suits. They were escorted to the district and reported to the People's Government for disposition. It was also learned that the 23rd Detachment of the Xianwater Public Security Bureau also seized 15 sacks of opium, each weighing more than ten catties, in the Lantouba area on the same day. It was reported that the well-known opium peddler Jiang Songyan from Jiangbei transported them from Hankou to the border area between Jiangsu and Anhui by steamer and then repackaged them for transport by sailing boat. The team has now detained the boat and confiscated the opium, but it is not known whether it will be transferred to the district for disposal.

There is still a white slip at the door stating "Strictly abide by the county government's mediation, and temporarily suspend the petition for another day to promote the attention of all sectors," signed "A Public Announcement by the Silk Fabric Shop Clerks." It is also learned that Fuyu Xiang and other fabric businesses have resumed normal operations. Dasheng opened on the morning of the 16th.

Wang, the daughter-in-law of Zou Changfu, a farmer in Qiaoshu Town in the seventh district of the county, is 29 years old. Since last autumn, her abdomen has been as big as a drum, and she thought it was bloating. Fortunately, her diet has remained constant and she has been living well, so she didn't care. Suddenly, around 1:00 p.m. on the 16th, she had labor pains and gave birth to a child with three heads and one body, with complete facial features. The whole town was shocked for a while, and the threshold of visitors was worn through. The family members regarded it as ominous and did not add swaddling clothes. It died after a while.

Hangzhou: The Jianggan Telephone Riot Expands 91

In the Jianggan District of Hangzhou, 131 households with South-character telephones were required by the Provincial Telephone Bureau to pay a machine deposit of 40 yuan per household by a deadline, otherwise their phones would be shut off and the machines removed. The users sent a letter to the bureau to question them, and a dispute arose. The telephone bureau began shutting off the phones of these households in order from the 17th. If they did not pay within ten days, all the machines would be removed. The situation is expanding. The users immediately elected representatives to form a committee to jointly deal with the situation and asked the chairman of the city's chamber of commerce, Wang Zhuzhai, and the manager of the Bank of China, Jin Runquan, to uphold justice. Mr. Wang immediately met with the director of the telephone bureau, Zhao Zengjue, at the Bank of China yesterday (the 18th) afternoon to discuss a solution. Zhao said that the machine deposit must be paid in accordance with the regulations, but the time could be considered. Installing automatic telephones is not possible due to economic reasons. The users, on the other hand, demanded that automatic telephones be installed, the same as in Gongbei and other places, and the machine deposit would be paid. Both sides' attitudes were quite firm, and a solution could not be reached immediately.

Local News

The Municipal Chamber of Commerce Requests the Implementation of Taxes on Japanese Rice Transported to Shanghai for Dumping 92

The Municipal Chamber of Commerce received a letter from the Ningbo Shanghai Fellow Association, stating that Japan recently had more than one million stones of stale rice, which are being dumped like a lotus. It is said that 25,000 stones will arrive in Shanghai soon. The association specially telegraphed the Ministry of Finance and the Ministry of Industry in Nanjing, requesting the implementation of taxes to save the declining countryside. The telegram is recorded as follows: To the Ministry of Finance and the Ministry of Industry in Nanjing, we have learned that Japan's stale rice is accumulated and the rice price is low, which has been reported many times. The situation is almost the same as in our country. Moreover, this year's new grain harvest in that country is said to be five to six million stones more than in previous years. It is really in the intention of using stale rice to dump in our country. Now the new grain in various provinces will be released soon. If foreign rice surges in, the price of new rice will be reduced. The tragedy of rural famine will be even worse than last year. Foreign rice tax has been rumored for a long time. It is heard that the Legislative Yuan has decided the tax rate. At this critical moment, the implementation should not be delayed. We request you to firmly preside over the matter and implement it as soon as possible. The Shanghai Municipal Chamber of Commerce bowed.

The Federation of Chambers of Commerce Cables the Government Requesting a Swift Draft of Foreign Rice Tax Rate 93

The National Federation of Chambers of Commerce cabled the Chen Government again yesterday, saying: To the Executive Yuan, Ministry of Foreign Affairs, Ministry of Finance, and Ministry of Industry of the Nanjing National Government, the imposition of a heavy import tax on foreign rice and the abolition of illegal donations on domestic rice to cure the rural economy, the above has been submitted to the Government for review. Later, Guangdong held a different opinion, and the association telegraphed the Guangdong Provincial Government, requesting a unanimous position. After that, Guangdong first implemented it, and Fujian followed suit. Since the two provinces have implemented the import tax on foreign rice, the needs of the two provinces of Guangdong and Fujian have caused the price to rise due to the lack of rice, and the savings of Hunan and Anhui provinces have seen activity and improvement. Although the time is not long, the effect has been significant. If our government can quickly implement it nationwide, its effectiveness will be even more remarkable. Then, after this autumn's harvest, farmers will be able to sell their surpluses. Although they cannot reach Suzhou immediately, they can get a little breather. Now, although our government's foreign rice tax principle has been passed by legislation, the rate of foreign rice tax is still to be drafted in detail by the Ministry of Finance. Generally, foreign rice merchants will take this opportunity to determine the tax rate and have not yet implemented the opportunity to fully transport and hoard to wait for selling. Then, when the new rice is on the market, it will inevitably be crowded out by foreign rice, and the decline in rice prices will be even more unimaginable. It is reasonable to cable the Chen Government again for review and earnestly request that the import tax rate on foreign rice be quickly drafted and implemented immediately. The National Federation of Chambers of Commerce bowed.

The Chinese People's Drug Elimination Society at 207 Mendelane Road, Shanghai, telegraphed the chairman of the Kuomintang, Lin Sen, the president of the Executive Yuan, Wang Jingwei, and the chairman of the Nanchang Military Commission, Jiang Jieshi, saying that Shanghai is a place where Chinese and foreigners gather, and it is also a hub for trafficking in drugs.
