The transportation method is quite mysterious. If you are not familiar with the inside story, it is not easy to find out. In Shanghai, there have been repeated seizures of large-scale manufacturing plants, and there are many newspaper records. However, no seizures have been made at stations and ports in the mainland. The reason is that the packaging of the drug is secret, and the carriers are cooperating with each other. Therefore, the traffickers of red pills feel more confident, and their flow is more practical than opium. Lin Zexu said that if this disaster is not eliminated, there will be no soldiers or salaries available in ten years. I am afraid that there will be no available people in the Republic of China in ten years. Thinking of this, I am deeply saddened. The members of our association have seen this and are deeply worried about the tragedy of the country's destruction and the extinction of the species. Therefore, this association was established to urge the government on the one hand and assist the authorities on the other hand, hoping to eliminate drugs and eliminate drug disasters, and to save the people from fire and water. This is what the members of our association pray for day and night. We have always admired your concern for the people's suffering and your hatred of evil. We dare to submit this to you for your review and approval to reiterate the ban, and to inform all places to transfer military and police agencies to secretly assist in the arrest, and especially pay attention to the Shanghai station. Our association is closer to the source and will report the handling at any time, so that the source can be eradicated and there will be a day when drugs can be eliminated. We also pray that you will comply with this order. The standing committee members of the Chinese People's Drug Elimination Society, Huang Jiemin, Qian Xuecheng, etc., bowed.

Beijing-Shanghai, Shanghai-Hangzhou-Ningbo, Tianjin-Pukou, Joint Transportation on Three Lines is Ready and Will Be Implemented on the 22nd of This Month. The Ministry of Railways Stipulates the Transportation of Luggage Fees 103

The opening of the joint transportation between Beijing-Shanghai, Shanghai-Hangzhou-Ningbo, and Tianjin-Pukou has been prepared and will be officially implemented on the 22nd of this month. The detailed rules for handling vehicles crossing the river and the fees for transporting luggage and packages by ferry have been stipulated by the Ministry of Railways. Yesterday, the Railway Bureau was ordered to comply with them. The details are recorded as follows:

Detailed Rules for Cross-River Vehicles 104

Detailed Rules for the Joint Operation of Cross-River Vehicles on the Jinpu, Jinghu, and Huhangyong Railways: Article 1. In addition to the regulations promulgated by the Ministry, these detailed rules shall apply to matters concerning the joint operation of vehicles crossing the river on the two railways. However, the rules for inspecting and repairing vehicles shall be formulated separately. Article 2. The two railways shall establish joint operation offices or stations to handle matters related to joint cross-river operations. The Jinghu Railway shall set up the Nanjing Jiangbian Joint Operation Station, abbreviated as DNT in English, and the Jinpu Railway shall set up the Pukou Joint Operation Office, abbreviated as PWT in English. Article 3. The joint operation offices and stations established by the two railways shall be jointly managed by one director or stationmaster, three clerks, one mechanical/engineering officer or vehicle inspector, two station attendants, and several craftsmen, all of whom shall be appointed by the respective railway bureaus' transportation and mechanical departments. Article 4. The Jinghu Railway shall use Nanjing Station as the passenger joint operation station and Nanjing Jiangbian Station as the freight joint operation station (goods arriving at Nanjing Station are treated the same as those arriving at Nanjing Jiangbian Station). The Jinpu Railway shall use Pukou Station as the passenger and freight joint operation station. Article 5. For joint operation of full carload or less-than-carload freight, and through trains between Shanghai and Ping, the handover station for verification and delivery of vehicles and goods shall be the joint operation office or station of the delivering railway. However, less-than-carload freight shall be transported by the delivering railway to the receiving railway's freight yard for unloading and reloading. Article 6. Except for through passenger trains between Shanghai and Ping, which shall be governed by separate regulations, the number of freight cars for joint operation between the two railways shall be determined by mutual agreement. The tonnage for crossing the tracks shall be temporarily limited to a load capacity of 2,000 tons. If the tonnage of vehicles crossing the tracks from Railway A reaches 2,000 tons and there are still freight cars to cross, Railway B may send empty cars to Railway A in exchange; otherwise, it shall be handled in accordance with Article 27 of the Provisional Measures, with self-unloading and reloading. In case of freight congestion, the two railways may negotiate separate solutions at any time. Article 7. The dispatching departments of the two railways shall contact each other at any time regarding the cross-river vehicles for joint operation. Article 8. Freight cars for joint cross-river operation shall be equipped with air brakes or complete hand brakes and shall be limited to eight-wheeled vehicles. Article 9. The handover procedures for joint cross-river vehicles shall be carried out during the ferry's working hours. However, the handover time shall be based on the ferry's departure time. Article 10. After the joint cross-river vehicles have been inspected, the director or stationmaster of the delivering railway shall fill out a vehicle handover notice, a through freight car route slip, and a joint freight delivery notice, and sign them together with all other joint freight documents, and hand them over to the receiving railway stationmaster or director for signature. Article 11. After the joint cross-river vehicles have been handed over, the director or stationmaster of the receiving railway shall send personnel with all the notices and documents to escort them across the river, except for through trains between Shanghai and Ping. Article 12. The director or stationmaster of the delivering railway shall record the vehicle number, type, railway, tonnage, total tonnage, number of vehicles, purpose of vehicle accessories, and origin and destination station names in detail in the vehicle delivery register for reference. Article 13. For joint cross-river vehicles that have not returned, the vehicle number, type, tonnage, number of vehicles, and tonnage shall be recorded in detail in the semi-monthly report, which shall be stamped by both parties. One copy shall be kept at the station, and one copy shall be sent to the Transportation Division of the Transportation Department for verification. Article 14. The cross-river track usage fees for joint cross-river vehicles shall be calculated by the number of passenger cars and by the tonnage of freight cars. Article 15. The joint operation offices and stations established by the two railways shall separately register and fill out delivery notices for joint cross-river vehicles and other non-joint cross-river vehicles for easy clearing. Article 16. The car rental and late fees for joint freight cars shall be handled in accordance with the regulations decided at the 16th National Joint Operation Conference and cleared by the Joint Operation Department of the Ministry of Railways. Article 17. For joint freight cars with Nanjing Station or Nanjing Jiangbian Station of the Jinghu Railway or Pukou of the Jinpu Railway as the destination station, no car rental shall be charged within 24 hours from the time of delivery. If it exceeds 24 hours but is less than 48 hours, car rental shall be charged. If it exceeds 48 hours, car rental and late fees shall be charged. However, in case of strong winds and heavy rain that make it impossible to unload the car, the time shall be deducted if approved by the other party. Article 18. Goods arriving at Pukou from Nanjing Jiangbian or Nanjing Station, or arriving at Nanjing Jiangbian or Nanjing Station from Pukou, shall not be processed for the time being. Article 19. If the Jinghu Railway uses returning empty vehicles, it may load less-than-carload freight to Bengbu and Xuzhou stations, one car per day for each station. The loading weight shall be calculated at least one-quarter of the car's tonnage, and the delivering party shall be responsible for handling the freight. Article 20. For south-bound joint operation less-than-carload freight sent to Pukou, the loading and unloading fees in Pukou shall be borne by the Jinpu Railway. For north-bound joint operation less-than-carload freight sent to Nanjing Jiangbian Station, the loading and unloading fees in Nanjing Jiangbian Station shall be borne by the Jinghu Railway. Article 21. The two railways shall send less-than-carload freight once a day at a specified time and each dispatch a car for joint circular use, without car rental charges. Article 22. If there are any matters not covered by these detailed rules, the responsible personnel of the two railways shall negotiate and submit them to their respective railway bureaus for revision and report to the Ministry for record. These detailed rules shall come into effect from the date of promulgation.

Transportation of Luggage and Parcels Fees 105

The Ministry of Railways instructed the Railway Bureau that the cargo crossing fees for the capital ferry and passenger fares had already been notified in the micro-telegram and the Lianzi No. 6724 order of this month, respectively, and should be followed. All cargo and passengers passing through the ferry should follow these regulations. The Ministry now stipulates the crossing fees for luggage and parcels transported by the capital ferry: 5 cents for every 20 kilograms of luggage (less than 20 kilograms will also be calculated as 20 kilograms), with a minimum charge of 10 cents; 3 li per kilogram for parcels, with a minimum charge of 10 cents. Once the fees for cargo, luggage, parcels, and passenger fares crossing the river have been set, no other donations or fees may be added, nor may they be reduced due to various discounted tickets. Those not crossing the river by ferry will still be handled according to the current methods. In addition, all through Shanghai-Ping passenger tickets and all tickets supplemented on the through Shanghai-Ping trains on the Beining, Jinpu, Jinghu, and Huhangyong railways should be printed with the four red characters "滬平通車" (Through Shanghai-Ping Train) to make them clear. A red horizontal line should be added above the four characters "滬平通車" to indicate that it includes the special express train surcharge. The procedures for supplementary tickets should be simplified. If tickets are supplemented en route, all fees from each railway and all supplementary fees should be collected at once to avoid each railway collecting fees separately and to save procedures. The crossing fees for all goods not graded and calculated by piece or item in the grading table will be notified separately after they have been successively determined. The above sections should be followed accordingly. The bureau has already instructed the Transportation Department to comply.

Hainan Sugar Merchant Representatives Plead for Assistance from Various Chambers of Commerce Yesterday 107

Xing Juefei, representative of the Qiongya sugar merchants of Guangdong and representative of the Haikou Chamber of Commerce, went to Beijing to petition about the Jianghai Customs' penalty on local sugar from Qiongya. Yesterday morning, Xing went to the National Federation of Chambers of Commerce and the Shanghai General Chamber of Commerce to request assistance. Xu Esheng, secretary of the Shanghai General Chamber of Commerce, received him, discussed the details of the situation and all the conclusive evidence, and stated that the chamber was paying close attention to the case, had previously telegraphed the Customs Administration three times to strongly argue the case, and would be willing to assist in handling it in the future. Lin Kanghou, chairman of the National Federation of Chambers of Commerce, also received him and stated that this matter was related to the life and death of the South China sugar industry and promised to do his best to assist. The Guangdong Shanghai Chamber of Commerce also convened a meeting yesterday afternoon at the request of Representative Xing, and the representative attended to report. It is reported that the representative will go to Beijing tonight. The details of the case stated by the representative are recorded as follows to clarify the truth of the case. In April of this year, seven businesses, including Liansheng in Haikou City, Qiongya, were penalized more than 6,000 yuan by the Qionghai Customs Commissioner for exporting local sugar, which was falsely represented as foreign sugar. The merchants were not convinced and transported the sugar to Shanghai to present it to the Jianghai Customs for re-verification. The result was that it was recognized as local sugar. Those who presented it to the Changsha Customs for re-verification were also issued verification documents. In May, the Qiong Guangdong and two other ships transported sugar from Haikou for export, and the Qiong Customs considered that it was mixed with foreign sugar, while the Jiang Customs considered it pure local sugar. In July, the Yongcheng and two other companies transported local sugar for export, and the Qionghai Customs Commissioner again pointed out that it was mixed with foreign sugar. The sugar merchants protested, and the commissioner could not show the difference between the local and foreign sugars. Later, the Haikou Chamber of Commerce mediated, and the commissioner allowed the sugar to be transported to Shanghai for re-verification. The commissioner did not quietly wait for the verification results, but secretly telegraphed the Jianghai Customs to indicate that the sugar was mixed with foreign sugar and requested that it be detained. The Jiang Customs did not investigate and approved the request. The sugar merchants felt wronged and repeatedly requested thorough investigation, but they were ignored. In the same month, two businesses, Housheng and others, transported local sugar to Shanghai, and both were repeatedly verified by the Qionghai Customs at the time of import and export, recognized as local sugar, completed tax payment according to regulations, and were released. When the goods arrived in Shanghai, they were detained by the Jiang Customs. The bad news came, and the sugar merchants in Shanghai were greatly shocked because the Qiong and Jiang Customs contradicted each other repeatedly, causing the merchants to suffer injustices and not know what to do. They had to decide to stop transporting to avoid losses and jointly asked more than 100,000 farmers who lived by producing sugar to ask the Qiongya authorities to maintain it. In this case, the Qiongya Pacification Commissioner Chen Zhangfu, Qionghai Customs Supervisor Zhan Jusi, Qiongya Industry Bureau Chief Zhu Yini, Qiongshan County Chief Chen Mengsun, and others all believed that the local sugar was hit by this blow, which was indeed a major economic crisis in Qiongya. They responded to the appeals of the city chamber of commerce and farmers and each sent representatives to a meeting to discuss ways to maintain local sugar to avoid the plight of farmers and merchants. Immediately after the resolution, representatives from the above-mentioned agencies were sent to form a local sugar field investigation team to personally inspect the sugar-producing areas in September in order to present to the central financial and economic departments to distinguish between the local and foreign sugars, and to effectively protect the Qiongya sugar industry. As a result, local sugar from Shizi Road Longchang and other places in Qiongshan County was brought back and publicly inspected in the city chamber of commerce. It was found that the local sugar in this area was the same as the local sugar previously detained in Shanghai. The Haikou City Chamber of Commerce and the sugar merchants then sent Xing Juefei as a representative to carry various physical evidences and written statements to Beijing to appeal to the central government to thoroughly investigate and redress the grievances suffered by the sugar merchants many times, and to effectively protect the safety of the export of local sugar in the area, so as to relieve the people's difficulties and revitalize the industry.

China Merchants Bureau Has Not Proceeded with Loan 108

According to the Central News Agency, the Ministry of Communications has approved the National China Merchants Bureau's plan to borrow 15 million yuan from the banking sector in the city. However, according to Liu Hongsheng, general manager of the bureau, the board of supervisors of the bureau has submitted a request to the Ministry of Communications for funds to be allocated to the bureau due to the lack of capital for business development. In addition, when the shares were repurchased, a temporary loan of about 3-4 million yuan was borrowed from the banking sector, so the 15 million yuan loan can only be used to repay the debts of the two places. Shanghai General Labor Union Issues Declaration, Sends Letter to Municipal Council, and Hosts Press Conference to Resolve the Electricity Strike 109

The strike by workers at the Shanghai Public Concession Electricity Company has now lasted more than 20 days. Although various parties have mediated, there has been no effect so far. If the company does not resolve this matter soon, the strike will expand, and the society will be affected. The Shanghai General Labor Union issued a declaration yesterday as a final appeal, sent a letter to the Board of Directors of the Municipal Council, and asked them to uphold justice and seek a swift resolution. It also hosted reporters from various newspapers at 3:00 p.m. The details are recorded as follows:

Declaration Issued Since the outbreak of the strike at the Public Concession Electricity Company, this union has deeply understood the importance of the public electricity business to society. On the one hand, it has persuaded workers to maintain the current so that the interests of social users are not affected. On the other hand, it has announced the details to all parties to seek a fair judgment. The report issued on the 9th of this month is even more detailed. This union's painstaking efforts to value public welfare should be understood by all parties. Now, the company insists on its preconceived ideas and does not make the slightest concession. Recently, it has hired a large number of White Russians to replace Chinese workers, making the workers who were forced to strike even more angry. Its lack of sincerity in reconciliation is obvious. We deeply regret this kind of action by the company. This union has examined the general situation and is deeply afraid that if it continues to insist, the workers will be forced by the needs of life, and when this union's advice loses its authority, a radical change will be inevitable, and all sectors of industry and commerce will suffer. Therefore, this union tirelessly tells our people from all walks of life that the cause of this strike seems to be the dismissal of three workers, but the crux of the problem is far beyond the company's continuous dismissal of workers over the years and the pension that the workers should have received. At first, the workers still hoped that the company would realize its mistakes, and only used patience and requests. When patience and requests were not enough to move the company's heart, the public was angered and the serious situation of today was formed. Since the electricity business is related to public welfare and social security, we seem unable to let it develop naturally until even more unfortunate events occur. In short, this union feels that it has exhausted its efforts and voices in dealing with this dispute. I hope that people from all walks of life, for the sake of the interests of users and the suffering of Chinese workers, will make a serious and powerful expression from the standpoint of supervising public utilities, so that the company authorities who adhere to preconceived ideas will know what to do. Society is fortunate, workers are fortunate. This declaration is made with respect.

Letter to the Municipal Council To the Shanghai Public Concession Municipal Council Board of Directors: Sirs, since the outbreak of the strike at the Shanghai Electricity Company, this union has been deeply afraid that this will lead to unfortunate events that may harm the public interest. In order to avoid the expansion of the situation, it has done its best to seek guidance or run around to find a way to mediate. Although representatives of the party and government, Shanghai General Chamber of Commerce Chairman Wang Xiaolai, and Chinese directors Yuan Ludeng and Xu Xinliu expressed their opinions to the company, they were rejected by the company authorities' preconceived and firm attitude. Even Mr. Zhong Si, the director of your bureau, offered his good intentions to mediate after the workers petitioned, but he did not receive the attention of the company authorities. The workers had no choice but to give a warning of a slowdown, and then the company's refusal to work led to the fact of a strike. However, the workers were fortunate to follow the advice of this union and continue to maintain the power generation work, which has not yet harmed the public interest. However, this kind of advice, whether its effectiveness can last, this union cannot estimate. Therefore, there are also meetings of social leaders to jointly maintain security and stability, and the publication of reports on resolving disputes, with the intention of obtaining a reasonable solution before the effect of the advice is exhausted. But waiting until today, the company, in addition to publishing an open letter that intends to insult and is not factual, has not shown any sincerity. There is no doubt that it is intentionally undermining the effectiveness of this union's advice and engaging in the manufacture of unfortunate events. Therefore, your council, in terms of its responsibility to manage municipal affairs and maintain security, cannot but pay attention to it. Therefore, this union has enclosed a copy of the report to all parties, a copy of the draft of the workers' rebuttal to the open letter, and asks your council to carefully review them and determine who is right and wrong. This union has already done its best to persuade the workers to make concessions on the conditions they demand, and has returned the judgment of whether the conditions for concessions are reasonable to the gentlemen who were previously enthusiastic about mediation. It is confident that it has done its best to respect justice and protect the public welfare of society. If this kind of fair and reasonable expression cannot make the company realize its mistakes, then the company's disregard for justice, disregard for municipal affairs, and disregard for the public welfare of helping it to benefit all users is also obvious. The company's current authorities, judging from their psychological views, are not suitable talents for operating a monopolized public utility. This council should immediately correct or advise its board of directors and the American headquarters to remove them for the sake of managing municipal affairs and maintaining public welfare and security. Otherwise, its past contempt for Mr. Zhong Si's psychology will inevitably advance to contempt for your council. Not only will your council's plans for citywide electricity and public welfare policies be obstructed, but it is feared that under its views of only knowing how to seek profit and oppression, an unfortunate event will be triggered, which is also likely to happen. If this kind of event becomes a reality, then from the point of view of municipal achievements, it will be a shame to record. This union knows that the efforts of advising striking workers are definitely not enough to resist the pressure of their livelihood needs. When this union's advice is exhausted, it will be the day when an incident occurs. Taking advantage of the fact that the strength has not yet been exhausted, this special request is made to your council, wishing your council to use its possible power to assist this union in preventing incidents, respecting justice, and the success of advocating the public welfare of society. Words cannot express everything. We respectfully await your reply.

Hosting Reporters The General Labor Union hosted reporters from various newspapers at 3:00 p.m. yesterday, and Zhu Xuefan reported on the progress of the strike, saying, in short, that the Public Concession Electricity Company has been on strike for more than 20 days. On the workers' side, because the electricity business is of great importance to social security, workers continue to work in the power generation section. On the company's side, although various parties have mediated, it has never accepted sincerity. On the workers' side, there are no preconceived ideas, and there are no so-called conditions. They only seek the upholding of justice and can resume work immediately. If this matter is not resolved quickly, so that the workers are forced to be unable to maintain, then once the power generation section is also declared to stop working, there will be a feeling of unease in the society, and the impact on factories will be even more serious. Since the January 28 Incident, the various Chinese factories in the city have been in a slump. Fisheries Merchants Association Telephones to Request Exemption from Pond Construction Fee Lists Ten Reasons for Requesting Exemption 110

In order to improve the entire Chinese fishery plan, the Ministry of Industry has established the Jiangsu-Zhejiang Fishery Improvement Committee and established the Fishery Collection and Construction Fee Office to work separately. Fishermen and merchants, unable to bear the burden, have successively presented petitions to the Ministry of Industry requesting exemption. After various mediations, the issue has been resolved. Now, the pond fresh fish merchants, on the grounds that the collection office uniformly collects 1% of river fresh and pond fresh, have aroused the opposition of the pond fresh fish merchants, and they have successively sent people to appeal to the authorities. Recently, the Shanghai Fisheries Merchants Association has presented a letter to the Ministry of Industry requesting an explanation of the difference between pond fresh and river fresh, requesting exemption, which is recorded as follows: Presentation regarding the request for exemption from the fishery construction fee for pond fresh fish. Since recent years, the economy of Chinese fishing villages has been extremely bankrupt, and the only thing that can survive is the absence of taxes and levies. Now, Your Excellency, in order to realize the entire fishery plan, has taken the initiative to collect fishery construction fees, revitalize the fishing village economy, and resist the intrusion of enemy fish. The good laws and good intentions are included in them, and our entire body of fishermen and merchants should sincerely support them. However, the uniform collection of river fresh and pond fresh is because Your Excellency has not understood the truth of the matter. We respectfully present it to Your Excellency. The fish harvested from Taihu Lake and the ocean are purely natural products, and fishermen do not need to raise them on weekdays. Pond fresh fish is not the same. They must be subject to field tax and surcharges. If pond fish is also levied, the indirect taxes and levies paid would be several times over. This is the first reason to request exemption. The fish body is collected from the Yangtze River area. Along the way, it is lost to extortion by military police and hooligans. Protectors cannot reach it in time, the cost is already heavy, and hope is difficult to expect. This is the second reason to request exemption. The fishing village economy has gone bankrupt, which is an undeniable fact. The funds for purchasing fish bodies are borrowed from banks, and after being exploited by heavy profits, they are also restricted by banks. Pond fish must be sold through banks, and each hundred yuan must pay bank commission of seven yuan. The number of one hundred yuan has lost fourteen yuan. Adding the profit to it, it is lucky that the cost is not eroded. This is the third reason to request exemption. The fish body enters the pond, and it takes three years of hard work to supply the market. There are field taxes, labor, and feed. Now, if the fish feed, such as snails, etc., must also pay construction fees, the cost of one fish is already insufficient. This is the fourth reason to request exemption. The grain fish raised and grown up is transported from the place of origin to the Shanghai market. Along the way, the military police and hooligans are again called "fish food" and forcibly demand a loss of 20%. Those in power may not have heard of it, but the fishermen and merchants suffer unspeakable pain. This is the fifth reason to request exemption. Each time a boat is berthed in Shanghai, it must pay a wharf fee of two yuan, which is deducted by the banks. If the weights and measures are eaten, the tails are owed, and the accumulation is small and the burden is heavy. This is the sixth reason to request exemption. What's more, in recent years, the rural areas have gone bankrupt, and vagrants are like crucian carp. There are thefts of fish and robberies of fish everywhere. The government has no special personnel to protect them, and fishermen are in great difficulty due to economic difficulties. The loss is huge. As for otters, frogs, kites, etc., the losses are also serious. It takes a lot of effort to get a fish to the market. This is the seventh reason to request exemption. What cannot be stopped from saying is that if there is a drought, the pond fish will not be left alive. If there is a flood, they will go with the waves. Not to mention fish plague and fish disease. This is the eighth reason to request exemption. What's more, the social economy has been fundamentally shaken, and red bandits are everywhere. Everywhere, they use the opportunity. If the fishermen have no way to make a living, how can they not take risks? If donations are doubled, their way to survival will be cut off. The hidden worries in the future are very anxious. This is the ninth reason to request exemption. The rural economy has gone bankrupt, and the government has begun to remedy it. The suffering of the fishermen should be measured by example. There is no time to save them. How can they be levied again? This is the tenth reason to request exemption. The above suffering is not dared to be silent. It is with the view of gathering firewood and the meaning of saints choosing them, and urgently speaking, hoping to examine the truth, condescendingly grant the request, and it is convenient for the public.

Silver Shops Installing Silver Furnaces: Ministry of Finance Orders All to be Dismantled; Unemployed Workers: Seven Already Employed by the Mint; Refinery to be Established for Mass Assessment and Recruitment 111

After the abolition of the tael and the adoption of the yuan, silver furnace businesses and public assaying bureaus were ordered to cease operations. Regarding silver furnaces installed in various silver shops,

the Ministry of Finance instructed the Silver Furnace Guild to notify them to dismantle all of them. The Central Mint is establishing a refinery to accommodate unemployed workers. The details are as follows:

Ministry of Finance Instructions 112

In addition to instructing the Money Guild to notify the silver furnace businesses and public assaying bureaus to cease operations, the Ministry of Finance also issued Instruction No. 9844, Qianzi, to the Shanghai Silver Furnace Guild, stating: It has been previously ordered that all silver furnaces in Shanghai must cease operations, dismantle the furnaces, and not privately open furnaces for melting and casting. Those silver shops in Shanghai that have silver furnace equipment must also dismantle all of them and not privately melt and cast silver for sale. This order is hereby issued for the guild to notify and ensure compliance. In the future, if any private furnace opening and melting is discovered, report the names immediately to the Ministry for investigation and handling. This order is issued.

Various Silver Shops Comply 113

After receiving the instructions from the Ministry of Finance, the Silver Furnace Guild forwarded them to the Shanghai Municipal Silver Shop Trade Association and the Shanghai Municipal New Silver Shop Trade Association for compliance. As for the approximately fifteen members of the Silver Shop Guild, namely the large silver shops, and the approximately sixteen members of the New Silver Shop Guild, namely the new silver shops, they have all been ordered to stop melting silver ingots. However, the approximately one thousand small shops, which have no organizational structure, usually also melted silver ingots in their business. Since the public assaying bureaus stopped assaying, although the silver furnaces have not been physically dismantled, they have also stopped melting silver ingots.

Recruiting the Unemployed 114

After receiving the order from the Ministry of Finance to assess and recruit unemployed workers from the silver furnace businesses and public assaying bureaus, such as those engaged in melting, testing, and assaying, the Central Mint, due to the need to hire more coinage workers, has already recruited seven unemployed workers from the Tongchu and Tongsheng silver furnace businesses. Furthermore, in view of the lack of equipment for refining silver to standard purity, the decision has now been made to establish a refinery. Preparations are underway, and unemployed workers from the silver furnace businesses and public assaying bureaus will be notified to go to the mint for performance assessment, so that they can be recruited as workers when the refinery begins operations.

Technical Cooperation Council's Board of Directors: Wu Yun-chu Elected Chairman, Hu Xi-yuan and Others Elected Standing Directors 115

The Technical Cooperation Council of Qian Yi Enterprise Silver Company held a board meeting at 5 PM yesterday. Directors Hu Xi-yuan, Xue Chun-sheng, Jin Run-xiang, Ren Shi-gang, Cheng Nian-peng, Wu Yun-chu, Zhang Hui, and others were present. Wu Yun-chu was elected chairman, and Hu Xi-yuan, Jin Run-xiang, Xue Chun-sheng, and Li Xin-fu were elected standing directors. The following procedural rules were resolved: (1) The Technical Cooperation Council of Qian Yi Enterprise Silver Company shall elect eleven

persons to form a board of directors according to Article 5 of the charter. (2) This board of directors shall handle all affairs of the Technical Cooperation Council in conjunction with Qian Yi Enterprise Silver Company. (3) The office of this board of directors shall be located in Qian Yi Enterprise Silver Company. (4) This board of directors shall mutually elect a chairman and four standing directors from among the directors. (5) When the Technical Cooperation Council and this board of directors hold meetings, the chairman shall be the ex officio chairman. If the chairman is absent due to business, another standing director shall be elected to act as chairman. Regular meetings and general meetings of the Technical Cooperation Council shall be convened by the board of directors. The board of directors shall be convened by the chairman. (6) The board of directors shall meet once a day. (7) Directors should attend each meeting on time. If they have unavoidable circumstances, they should entrust one of the other directors to represent them. Each director is limited to representing one person, and the voting right is still limited to the director himself. If a director is absent for three consecutive meetings without reason, the alternate candidate with the next highest number of votes shall fill the vacancy. (8) Resolutions of the board of directors shall be based on the number of people. Resolutions shall be voted on with the consent of more than half of the directors present. If the number of votes is the same on both sides, the chairman shall decide. If all the opposing members object, the meeting may be adjourned once. The resolution of the adjourned meeting cannot be opposed again by any party. (9) Regarding production, marketing, economic assistance, and other beneficial matters of the members of the Technical Cooperation Council, the board of directors may propose and pass them at any time, and then request Qian Yi Enterprise Silver Company to handle them.

The Tragic Situation of Banditry in Taihe County: The County Has Been Ravaged Five Times 121

Taihe County in Anhui Province has suffered severely from banditry. The Red Swastika Society has sent personnel to provide relief. However, the disaster area is vast and the number of disaster victims is large. It is not enough to raise funds extensively to save the dying people. Yesterday, the county sent representatives Gao Ji-zhi and Xu Ming-ya, with letters and photos of the disaster area, to the Red Swastika Society, requesting continued relief. The words were tragic. The original letter is excerpted below: Respected Sirs, Taihe is a poor and barren land. It has always been without reserves. In addition, there have been two years of poor harvests, and nine out of ten households are empty. Fortunately, there was timely rain and sunshine, and there was hope for the autumn harvest. Unexpectedly, on August 13, more than 10,000 bandits from Cheng, Yang, Jiang, and Ma suddenly occupied the old county seat of Jiuxianji in this county from Wenji and Huaji in Fuyang. They occupied it for ten days, and every day they went out to burn, kill, rob, and plunder, to the west to Shuizipu, Jieshouji, Chenmiaoji, and Mengji, to the south to Zhuanqiaoji, to the east to Yuanqiangji and Anfengji, and to the north to Gaomiaoji, Shuangfu, and Black Tiger Temple. On the 24th, they passed through Caimiao and Dahuangmiao to the vicinity of Guangwumiao and Lixingji, and occupied it for three days. This is the first time they passed through and ravaged the area. On August 28, they passed through Guangwumiao and Lixingji, and then Shuangmiao, Zhangcedian, Banqiaoji, and Zitaiji towns, and then sneaked into the two counties of Wo and Meng. This is the second time they passed through and ravaged the area. On September 2, they sneaked back from Wo and Meng, passing through Feihekou, Pugouji, Hongshanmiao, Qingniquan, Cishengji, Qiuquji, Shicao, and the two counties, and then sneaked into the Meiludian area in Henan Province. This is the third time they passed through and ravaged the area. On September 7, they sneaked back from Henan to Guangwumiao, passing through Hujiji, Ganggouji, Niqiuji, Quanqiaodian, Maji, Minglidian, Yuanqiangji, Santaji, Renzumiao, and Shuangheji, and then occupied Cihepu in Fuyang County. This is the fourth time they passed through and ravaged the area. On September 9, the Huo Xiao bandits sneaked from Longwangtang and Huaji in Fuyang to Shuizipu and Caimiao Dahuangmiao, and occupied them for three days. They passed through Lixingji and Cishengji, and then broke through the city of Luyi County in Henan Province. This is the fifth time they passed through and ravaged the area. In total, these five occupations and raids lasted for more than a month. The burning and slaughtering exceeded those of Chuang and Xian. Wherever the iron horse stepped, every family fled for their lives like bees. The ropes pulled, and wave after wave of people were driven like pigs. The fire of the dark wind consumed food and houses, leaving nothing behind. The banners of opposition to Japan were raised, but the livestock and people were already without survivors. The bones were scattered across the fields, and the blood flowed into ditches. The sad and tragic sights were unbearable to speak of. The entire county is only about a hundred li wide, and it has been ravaged by bandits and turned into scorched earth. Now that the golden wind is blowing and the jade dew is falling, it is evident that hundreds of thousands of disaster victims will have no home, no clothes to keep warm, and no food to eat. They will surely freeze and starve to death. Our association witnessed this and was heartbroken and disturbed. We have decided to raise funds locally and find ways to rescue them. However, the disaster is serious and the number of refugees is large. A drop in the bucket is not enough to solve the problem. Therefore, we have specially appointed Chen Xia-fu and

Gao Ji-zhi to go to your esteemed association to make a sincere appeal, hoping that you will extend your benevolent kindness to save the disaster victims. Then those who accumulate good deeds will surely have more blessings, and those who receive grace will never forget the favor. Looking forward to your kindness, we will be extremely grateful. Taihe County Bandit Disaster Relief Committee, Zhang Zemin, representative, Gao Ji-zhi, Chen Xia-fu,

Taihe County burial team working at Wangwan etc.

Workers from the Sanyou Factory Petitioned the District Court Yesterday: Requesting the Enforcement of the Municipal Government's Ruling 122

The labor dispute at the Sanyou Industrial Company's main factory in Pudong, since the Municipal Government organized an arbitration committee last year, has resulted in the employer filing a lawsuit. The lawsuit was rejected in all three trials. In April of this year, the Supreme Court sent the case to the Shanghai District Court for enforcement in accordance with the arbitration ruling. Although the court has summoned both parties for reconciliation more than ten times, it has been to no avail because the employer has no sincerity. The workers, considering that the employer is as stubborn as ever and that the court is delaying enforcement, and with autumn turning into winter, are extremely anxious about the future. Yesterday morning at 10:00 AM, the workers specially sent representatives Ni Zhong-yu, Sun Shou-ming, Kuang Wen-long, and others, more than a hundred people, holding petition banners and wearing symbols, to petition the District Court in formation. First, the representatives stated their opinions, saying that the Sanyou labor dispute was sent to the court for enforcement in April of this year, and it has been six months. Since the other party is stubbornly unrepentant, they requested the court to enforce the law as soon as possible. The court representative expressed acceptance and introduced the judge in charge of the case, Pang Shu-rong, to meet with them so that they could fully express the court's main purpose regarding this case. Judge Pang then said that the court hoped that both parties would reach a voluntary settlement, but it was not fulfilled. He expressed that the court would enforce the law in accordance with the schedule on the 24th of this month and asked everyone to wait patiently. The representatives considered it satisfactory and returned.

Bloody Incident Occurs at the Intersection of Pinlang Road: Two Workers Encounter Thugs After Work: Thug Shot Dead on the Spot by Constable 124

Yesterday afternoon at around 5 PM, a case of attempted mass murder, resulting in the wounding of a constable and the shooting death of the assailant on the spot, occurred at the intersection of Pinlang Road at the end of Xiao Shadu Road. A description of the situation follows:

Thugs Lie in Wait to Commit Crime 125

Workers Yan Cheng-bao and Xu Fu-zhang both work at a factory on Pinlang Road and are very close friends, going in and out together. There is also a labor hospital located near the Maode Lane nearby. At around 5 PM yesterday afternoon, just as various factories were letting out workers, six or seven men suddenly came to the entrance of the Maode Lane labor hospital, hiding in the lane, seemingly with intentions. However, since there were no actions at the time, it was impossible to know their intentions. When the factories sounded their whistles to let out workers, Yan and Xu left the factory together and walked home. When they reached the entrance of Maode Lane, one of the men hiding in the lane suddenly rushed out and blocked Yan's path. At the same time, the rest of the gang swarmed up and surrounded Yan. The man who had blocked the path then raised a pre-prepared axe and chopped it down at Yan.

A Fellow Worker Takes the Blow 126

However, Yan had great strength and, seeing that things were not going well, quickly used his right hand to parry the axe handle, took the opportunity to jump out of the encirclement, and ran away, shouting for help. Xu Fu-zhang was still behind Yan. Seeing this, he also ran forward to chase the assailant. Because they were about a dozen yards away, the assailant noticed Xu early. Taking advantage of Xu's unpreparedness, he turned around and chopped at Xu with the axe. As a result, Xu's head was struck by the axe, and he immediately fell to the ground. The assailant then chopped again at Xu's foot and tried to escape. Xu screamed in pain, which was heard by Constable No. 1083 nearby. The constable rushed to the scene and, seeing the situation, quickly drew his gun and gave chase. When he caught up, the assailant was extremely violent.

Assailant Shot Dead on the Spot 127

He turned around and fought the constable with the axe. The other gang members also surrounded the constable from all directions, trapping him in the center, and tried to seize his gun. The constable fought bravely against them. The thugs, seeing that they could not succeed, the assailant with the axe chopped at the constable's left hand. After being injured, the constable quickly fired three shots at the assailant who was committing the crime and resisting arrest. He was shot dead on the spot. The rest of his accomplices fled for their lives, so they were not captured. The injured constable quickly took a car back to the Putuo Road police station to report the incident. A large number of detectives were dispatched to search and pursue the gang. At the same time, Xu Fu-zhang, who was injured in the line of duty, was rushed to the hospital for treatment. However, Xu's injuries were very serious, and his life was not yet assured. The body of the assailant who was shot dead on the spot has been taken to the morgue for examination. Afterwards, Yan Cheng-bao also went to the Putuo Road police station to report the facts of the incident, and said that he recognized the dead assailant as Wang Chang-gui, a reactionary element among the workers. Wang had incited labor unrest in the past, which was discovered and reported by Yan, and therefore held a grudge and committed this crime.

Shanghai Municipal Police Department: Busts a Gambling Den in Zhabei: Grand Scale, Luxurious Furnishings: Millions Wagered Nightly: Informed by Someone, Officers Dispatched to Arrest: Police Officers Disguised as Gamblers 128

--The boss, Chen Qian-yi, one name, 19 gamblers, gambling equipment, and three cars seized on the spot--

Recently, the Shanghai Municipal Police Department suddenly received a tip that Chen Qian-yi, a well-known gangster and gambler from Guangdong, and others in Zhabei, within the jurisdiction of the Second Precinct of the Fifth District, had recently pooled money to establish a large-scale gambling den at No. 10 Anning Lane, Zhongzhou Road. The furnishings inside were extremely luxurious, with roulette, pai gow, and Sic Bo, everything was available, and many greeters were hired to socialize with the gamblers. Therefore, every evening when the lights came on, there were shadows and bustling activity, with people and vehicles coming and going. Those entering and leaving were all upper-class figures. Millions were wagered nightly, and the smoke-filled couches were filled with people blowing smoke and shouting all night long. However, because it was handled properly, it has not been busted until now. After Commissioner Wen learned of this, he sternly ordered the Inspection Division the day before yesterday to assign two inspectors and eight police officers from the police brigade, carrying weapons, to go undercover to make arrests. After receiving the order, the officers drove to the location of the gambling den at around 8 PM the night before last, disguised as gamblers to enter. However, because it was too early, there were few gamblers. The officers then arrested the boss, Chen Qian-yi, and 19 gamblers, including Zhu Kang-you, along with various gambling equipment, smoking equipment, and roulette wheels, loaded them onto three trucks, and took them back to the headquarters. After Commissioner Wen interrogated them, he ordered that the arrested criminals be temporarily detained and then handed over to the Third Section for separate strict handling. Meanwhile, he continued to send officers to pursue the important fugitives from the gambling den who were at large.

Verdict in the Murder Case of the Dismembered Body in Baiyangzhai, Wusong 129

--The murderer, Gu Fu-tao, sentenced to life imprisonment--

Gu Fu-tao, a farmer from Baiyangzhai on the border of Baoshan County in northern Wusong, killed his wife because his wife, Xiao-mei, was having an affair with Long A-gou, which caused a widespread scandal. Fu-tao secretly found out the details and had thoughts of murder. Then, on the night of July 1, while his wife was fast asleep, he killed her with an axe. He then dismembered the body into ten pieces, stored them in a wooden bucket, and hid them in the woodpile in the wall. He planned to escape alone the next morning at dawn. However, he was discovered by neighbors, who stopped him halfway and took him to the Baoshan County government. This was reported in this newspaper on July 3. It is now learned that the case was repeatedly interrogated by the judge He Rui-lin sent by County Magistrate Jin, and the adulterer Gong A-gou was also arrested. Gu Fu-tao admitted without hesitation that he killed his wife with an axe and dismembered her. Yesterday, the verdict was announced. The defendant, Gu Fu-tao, dismembered and killed a person, and should be punished in accordance with Article 284, Paragraph 1, Item 2 of the Criminal Law. However, it was found that the defendant's personality was usually kind, and the motive for his crime was indeed provoked. After considering the circumstances, there is a reason for leniency. One-third of the original sentence should be reduced in accordance with Article 77 of the same law, and in accordance with Article 79, Paragraph 2 of the same law, he should be sentenced to life imprisonment. The adulterer Gong A-gou was sentenced to six months' imprisonment for having consensual intercourse with a married woman.

A Teenager Commits Suicide in Lao Dafang Inn 130

--The deceased was named Wu Lian and suffered from economic hardship--

At around 6 PM the day before yesterday, a teenager suddenly checked into the Lao Dafang Inn at No. 55 Puqing Lane, Fujian Road in the Public Concession. He claimed to be named Wu Lian. The inn's accountant opened Room 33 for him. After the tea server brought in tea and water, the teenager closed the door and went to sleep. However, at around 12 PM yesterday, the tea servers saw that the teenager had not yet gotten up, so they knocked on the door and called him, but there was no response for a long time. They became suspicious and asked a carpenter to find a way to open the door and enter. They then saw the teenager lying stiffly in bed, with a pale face and liquid gurgling out of his mouth. His breathing was as faint as a thread. They knew that he had taken poison and immediately reported it to the Lao Zha Police Station. A car was dispatched to send him to Renji Hospital for treatment. However, because the poison had taken too deep, he could not be saved and died. The hospital notified the police station, who transferred the body to the morgue to be examined. The court was notified to conduct an examination this morning, and a suicide note was found on the deceased's body, stating that he had taken this action because he was suffering from economic hardship. The clothes he was wearing were a free cloth long gown, suit pants, gauze underwear, woolen shirt, yellow leather shoes, and felt hat. Other than that, he had no other possessions. The police station is currently investigating the relatives of the deceased.

Gambling Den Busted: Gamblers Punished Separately 131

The premises at No. 536 Sichuan Road and Beijing Road, recently rented and opened as a gambling hall by Liang Gui-hua from Guangdong, was exceptionally large in scale and well-equipped. There were more than 60 gamblers every day. The house was three stories high. The second floor was divided into three rooms, set up as gambling halls. The third floor was the total gambling room, reading and exchanging chips, calculating the gains and losses of the gamblers. Day and night, it was merry and high-spirited, with very large winnings and losses. However, in order to avoid the attention of the police authorities, a bronze plaque was hung at the door, with the words "Yue Zhuang Xiang Fa Hao" written on it, pretending to be a commercial firm. On the back of the bronze plaque, the eight characters of "Five Direction Kings, Land Lords, and Gods of Wealth" were engraved, which were used as a secret sign to instruct gamblers. It was discovered by the General Police Headquarters. At 10:10 PM the day before yesterday, detectives Lu Gen-sheng, Zhang Ming-de, inspector Geng De-biao, Liu Xiang-zhai, and constables Li Wen-bin and Zhang Xiao-lin were ordered to secretly go to the address to arrest them. The boss Liang Gui-hua, the bookkeeper Wang Si, Zheng Jiu, and the gamblers Luo Xuan, Zhou Tang, Feng Qing, Zhen Han-ping, Zhang Lin, Xiao Quan, Gao He, and Chen Wei (all from Guangdong), totaling 25 people, were arrested. Gambling equipment, pai gow dice, and other gambling money worth more than 130 yuan, as well as chips and gambling books, were seized and taken back to the police station. Yesterday morning, they were sent to the First Special Court. The police station's lawyer, Qian Xun-jiu, prosecuted them in accordance with Articles 180 and 278 of the Criminal Law. After Judge Huang Ri-sheng interrogated the defendants, he sentenced Liang Gui-hua to two months' imprisonment and fined him 400 yuan. Wang Si and Zheng Jiu were each sentenced to one month's imprisonment and fined 60 yuan. The others were each fined 30 yuan. The gambling equipment and gambling money were all confiscated.

Murderer Wang Xu-qing Tried in Court Yesterday 132

--Accomplices Still Need to Be Arrested, Postponed for Seven Days--

Zheng Jin-long, a gangster (nicknamed Old Goods Jin-long) who lived at No. 3 Sanxin Lane, Dagu Road, had a feud with his fellow gangster Wang Xu-qing (nicknamed Little Master) due to gambling. Wang, at 6:40 AM on July 31 last year, gathered two accomplices, each holding a pistol and axe, and broke into Zheng's house. Without asking why, they chopped at Zheng indiscriminately. As a result, Zheng was struck by nine axes and fell to the ground seriously injured. The assailants fled in a rush. After someone reported it to the Xin Zha Police Station, Zheng was sent to Baolong Hospital for treatment. The court was requested to issue a warrant for the arrest of Wang Xu-qing. However, Wang knew that the situation was urgent after the incident and that he could not stay in Shanghai, so he left Shanghai for Wuhan. After a year, he thought that the situation had cooled down and that the matter had been forgotten, so he secretly returned to Shanghai and hid in the French Concession. However, he was discovered by detective Zhu Meng-wei and officer Hang Fa-lin of the Xin Zha Police Station. At noon the day before yesterday, they secretly went to Klock Road in the French Concession, disguised as laborers, and waited. Before long, Wang Xu-qing came face to face, and they arrested him and took him back to the Xin Zha Police Station. Yesterday morning, he was sent to the Eighth Criminal Court of the First Special District. The police station's lawyer, Wang Yao-tang, described the case and requested that the case be postponed so that the accomplices could be arrested. The defendant Wang Xu-qing admitted that the matter was done together with his accomplices Huang Dou, Lao Er, and the little hooligan A-jin and others, and that he was holding an axe at the time. Lawyer Fan Gang was hired to defend him in court. After Judge Xue Lan-ru verified the confession, he ordered Wang to be detained pending investigation and re-examination of the accomplices in seven days.

Hsieh Lung Tobacco Company Robbery Case: Four Robbers Arrested 133

On the evening of the 13th of this month, at 8:30 PM, the Hsieh Lung Tobacco Company at 763 Niu Chuang Road was suddenly invaded by five or six armed bandits, who robbed more than 2,000 dollars in cash. Huang Yongji, the Chinese detective chief of the Mixed Court Police Station, and detective Tao Afu, learned that the gang of robbers was hiding at 375 Zhoujiazuilu Road in a "tiger stove" (a public stove), secretly gathering and plotting, and also peeking at the business situation of a certain hardware store across the street, hoping to rob it. Therefore, at 4:30 PM the day before yesterday, they secretly went to the location with Western detectives and arrested Wu Tianxiu and Han Changli, both from Zhenjiang. Afterwards, they went to room 22 of the Yu Tong Hotel on Hanzhong Road in Zhabei, together with the Public Security Bureau, and arrested two more accomplices, Chen Guangrong, a man from Jiangbei, and a woman, Dong Heshi. They were taken to the police station one after another and escorted to the Eighth Criminal Court of the First Special District Court yesterday morning. Judge Wu Tingqi presided over the interrogation. Wang Yaotang, the police station's lawyer, stated the facts of the case, saying that the defendants confessed in the police station that they were involved in the robbery of the Hsieh Lung Tobacco Company. Wu Tianxiu was outside acting as a lookout at the time, and although Han and Chen did not go to the robbery together, they were both present during the discussion. Dong Heshi was the one who privately transported the stolen firearms. Therefore, the case still needs to be investigated, and he requested permission to postpone the hearing. Judge Wu questioned the defendants and ordered them to be detained separately and the hearing rescheduled for further investigation.

Illegal Sale of Tobacco Lottery Tickets Case Scheduled for Sentencing 134

Lu Yaojiang, a native of Haimen, opened the Da Shun Tobacco and Paper Store at No. 79 Dongxinqiao Street in the French Concession. Recently, he had a strange idea: he swapped the cigarette packs of various tobacco companies for lottery tickets and sold them at the store for 120 cash each. He also prominently displayed a sign in front of the store advertising the sale of these lottery tickets, which attracted the attention of passersby. Many people who wanted to get rich rushed to the store to buy them, and business was quite good. The French police found out and, believing that his private sale of lottery tickets violated the regulations of the Municipal Council, sent detectives to the store the day before yesterday and confiscated 1,372 Binlang brand cigarette lottery tickets, 597 Hongyun brand cigarette lottery tickets, 144 Haole brand tickets, and many other tickets such as Gaoerfu, Xuangong, Sanhua, Sanbei, Hongshi, and Da Lian Zhu. The shop owner Lu Yaojiang and his assistant Rong Fanrong were arrested and taken to the police station. Yesterday, they were escorted to the Eighth Criminal Court of the Second Special District Court. Judge Qiu interrogated them. First, the police station's lawyer Yao Zhaodi stated the facts of the case and presented the lottery tickets. Lu and Rong, the two defendants, admitted to illegally selling cigarette lottery tickets in violation of the regulations. The court ordered the closing of the debate and scheduled the sentencing for the 21st. The defendants were returned to custody to await instructions.

Four Robbers Apprehended at the Gongping Road Wharf 135

Liu Baoshan, a Chinese detective of the Wayside Police Station, and a Western detective, apprehended four robbers, Wang Yulin (a local), Sun Hongshan (from Jiading), and Jin Arong (from Suzhou), at the Gongping Road Wharf on Broadway Road at around 3:00 AM the day before yesterday. They found a handgun and ten bullets on Wang. After questioning them, they learned the location where their accomplices were hiding and went to room 215 of the Yingbin Hotel at 21 Zhejiang Road, where they arrested another suspect, Cao Zhangqing, from Tongzhou. They were all escorted to the Third Criminal Court of the First Special District Local Court yesterday morning. The police station's lawyer Zhang Tianyin stated the circumstances of the arrest, saying that the investigation revealed that the defendants were repeat offenders with a record of robbery convictions. They were planning to rob a resident's property on Gongping Road, but fortunately, the detectives learned of their plan and apprehended them. He requested permission to detain them and presented the gun and bullets for inspection. Wang Yulin confessed that he and Jin Arong had crossed the Huangpu River from Pudong and landed at the Gongping Wharf, intending to find his friend Zhou Yilong, who was a foreman at the Yihe Yarn Factory. He met Cao Zhangqing on the way, who said he urgently needed to defecate and asked Wang to temporarily hold the handgun for him. Unexpectedly, they were caught by the Chinese and Western detectives. Wang also hired lawyer Fan Gang to defend him. Sun Hongshan confessed that he knew Jin Arong and wanted to visit a friend at the Caojiadu Yarn Factory, but was arrested on the way. Cao Zhangqing confessed that a Japanese person had asked him to take the handgun to the Yangshupu Bridge for four dollars, and he asked Wang to carry it for him, which was the truth. Judge Wu Zehan ordered the defendants to be detained and the hearing rescheduled.

Municipal Health Bureau: Free Smallpox Vaccination 136

The Municipal Health Bureau, in accordance with the Ministry's order and the Central Vaccination Regulations, designates March to May and September to November each year as the spring and autumn vaccination periods. However, the Bureau wants to adapt to local conditions and may advance or extend the vaccination time as needed. The Bureau has specially consulted with registered hospitals and doctors in the city to entrust them to set up preventive vaccination branches, responsible for providing free vaccinations within the Bureau's designated vaccination period, and reporting the number of vaccinations to the Bureau for statistics on a monthly basis. On the other hand, the Bureau will organize its own vaccination teams to be dispatched to schools, factories, and other public and private organizations throughout the city. At the same time, personnel will be sent to bustling traffic areas to set up booths to provide vaccinations, with special attention to concentrated slum areas. Now that autumn is deep and smallpox is about to become epidemic, the Bureau has started to vaccinate students in primary and secondary schools in the city since September 15th. As of today, more than 36,000 people have been vaccinated. After the vaccination of schools is completed, factories and citizens will be vaccinated. The locations for free smallpox vaccination are listed below: Shanghai Municipal Health Bureau (Maojia Lane, Nanshi), Municipal South Clinic (Yudeli Intersection, Penglai Road), Public Shi Hai Hospital (Duojia Road, Nanshi), Waterside Pavilion Free Clinic (Waterside Pavilion Intersection, Nancang Street, Nanshi), Nanyang Hospital (Huangjia Road, Xiaonanmen, Nanshi), Women and Children Hospital (Fangxie Road, Nanshi), Taizhou Hospital (Xinyang Street, Minguo Road), Shenzhou Hospital (Baoxiangli, Zhaojiabang Road, Nanshi), Children's Free Clinic (Wuzhen Road, Zhabei), Chinese Public Hospital (Tongji Road, Zhabei), Hongkou Civilian Maternity Hospital (behind the Tilanqiao Police Station), Shanghai Epidemic Hospital (Aiduya Road, Xizang Road), Labor Hospital (Xiaoshadu Road), Huxi Commune (Roberts Road), Sino-German Maternity Hospital, Zhengyi Society, Jing'an Temple Road, Zhangjiabang (Huade Road, Dalianwan Road), Tongde Hospital (Tongfu Road), Hongkou Skin Disease Hospital (173 Linping Road).

According to yesterday's Japanese-language Shanghai Daily, Mr. Koji Matsumoto, the owner of the Matsumoto Parking Company on Zhapu Road in this city, returned to Japan on the Nagasaki Maru on the 11th. On the afternoon of the 14th, when the ship arrived in Kobe, he was suddenly found dead from taking sleeping pills. It is said that he committed suicide because he was burdened with debts of 20,000 yuan. Matsumoto had been in Shanghai for nearly four years. Since the outbreak of the Shanghai Incident, his automobile business has been quite successful. In less than three years, his profits reached 30,000 yuan. During the incident, the Japanese side did not have enough cars, and Matsumoto was able to cope with the situation by using Chinese merchants. He also worked as a driver at the Consulate General and was a well-known figure in the Japanese automobile business. Later, due to expansion, he lost more than 20,000 yuan and fell into a state of neurasthenia, so he committed suicide by taking sleeping pills.

The World News Agency reports that Dharma Teacher Xiangwen, a great master of Esoteric Buddhism and Chairman of the Chinese Zhuzang Esoteric Vehicle Juehua Society, traveled around various places in 1929, promoting Esoteric Dharma. After returning to Sichuan, he founded the Esoteric Buddhist Lay Forest in Chengdu, and established the Liren Charity Association, providing medicine and materials, and providing relief to widows and the poor. He has been tireless in promoting the Dharma and benefiting living beings. He will choose a date to transmit the Dharma. After a short rest, he plans to go to Putuo and Hangzhou to worship the Buddha and sightsee.

Fulun Twin Palace Silk Factory Workers Resumed Work Yesterday Morning, But Struck Again in the Afternoon 141

The case of the strike by workers at the Fulun Heng Twin Palace Silk Factory at the bottom of Hongkou Baolu has had many twists and turns. Here is the news from yesterday:

Resumption of Work: The workers of the Fulun Twin Palace Factory went on strike on the afternoon of the 6th because they opposed the strict management of Shen Xiangqing, the manager of the factory. After mediation by the Social Affairs Bureau on the 16th, it was recognized that the workers' strike was not in accordance with the rules, and the capital was ordered to not be too strict in its management. It was agreed that work would resume the next day, and the dispute would be resolved. Yesterday morning at 5:45, the factory sounded the whistle to start work in order to comply with the orders of the Social Affairs Bureau. At that time, only half of the workers arrived, and they stood at the factory gate without entering immediately. After the factory manager personally persuaded them, they went to work inside.

Strike Again: When the factory started work, the Fourth District Silk Industry Union sent people to supervise again. The factory asked the union to persuade the 200 workers who did not report to work as scheduled to return to work in the afternoon. However, not only did the number of people not increase after the lunch break, but the workers who were already working also went on strike again. The factory has decided to continue to start work this morning and pay the wages for this month. If the workers still do not resume work, it will temporarily shut down in order to make the workers realize their mistake, and plans to petition the party and government agencies to severely punish the instigators of the strike.

Creating the Content of the Rose Garden New Village 142

Shanghai is the most prosperous city in the country, but it is also very troublesome. Those who live here often suffer from working hard all day and have difficulty finding a place to rest. Moreover, the rent is surprisingly high, and most of the monthly income is spent on rent, but it is still narrow and difficult to live in, which is really regrettable. New village projects are most popular in European and American countries, but in our country, although there have been proposals, few have been implemented. Recently, entrepreneurs such as Mr. Zhang Yongnian initiated the organization of the China New Village Construction Society. First, 100 acres of land will be opened up in West Shanghai to build the Rose Garden New Village. The environment is beautiful and the scale is grand. The perfection of the design is unmatched in the East and West. Its facilities not only solve the problem of housing, but also have detailed plans for children's education, women's employment, etc. The village has a community center, primary school, kindergarten, home assistance group, family craft room, sports field, etc., to create a complete family. The standard of living is standardized and the economy is rationalized. What is even better is that anyone who joins the village can choose to build according to the house plan they have prepared, and the land price and construction costs can be paid in installments, like paying for a house. This not only avoids the difficulty of raising a large sum of money to buy property, but also compared to renting a house and paying a large amount of rent every month, no matter how many years later, the house still belongs to the landlord, which is much cheaper. The picture on the left is one of the house plans in the new village, designed by architect Qian Changgan. The A-type house, including land price, construction cost, and equipment such as flowers, trees, and lawns, costs a total of 9,000 yuan. Those who want to join can directly contact the China New Village Construction Society at 20 Bowuyuan Road.

The Twenty-Fifth District Branch of the Shanghai Citizens' Federation on North Sichuan Road held a meeting yesterday. All executive members attended and elected Wei Langxuan as chairman. The meeting was held as usual. The purpose of the meeting was reported and the agenda was announced. The following was discussed: (1) Secretary Guan Jichuan proposed that the previous committee intended to provide 10,000 yuan in relief funds to disaster-stricken merchants in the district in principle, and the method of distribution has been reported to the Public Security and Finance Bureaus and forwarded to the Municipal Government for approval. Now it intends to formulate detailed rules and regulations, and requests a public decision on the case. It was resolved to pass the proposal. (2) Four members, including Li Guangyu, Yucheng, and Changsheng, followed the Municipal Government's regulations and paid the housing donation on behalf of the Shengshan Zhen paid the housing donation on behalf of the owner, deducting the original housing donation from the rent. Negotiations have been ignored. Therefore, it is requested that assistance be provided. It was resolved to send a letter to the Public Security Fifth Sub-bureau and transfer it to the Finance Bureau for handling. (3) More than 20 households of members in North Fengleli jointly applied because the water supply in the area has been cut off by the owner, China Business Leasing Company, since July 14. During the three meetings, only drinking water was supplied for one day. Its methods are bad and its intentions are sinister (the court's files can be checked). It is requested that the local authorities be called upon to restore the water source and compensate for the loss of purchasing water. It was resolved to first submit a request to the Municipal Government, the Municipal Party Department, the Health Bureau, and the Public Security Bureau to quickly restore drinking water and attach importance to the livelihood of the people. (4) The association's finances are strained. It was resolved to collect membership fees to subsidize the association's affairs. The meeting was adjourned after the discussion.

Young Woman Commits Suicide by Poisoning After Argument with Husband 146

Mrs. He Yan, a young woman from Ningbo, was 23 years old and lived at No. 6 Dingxiangli, Yulihe Road, behind the abattoir in the French Concession. Her husband used to be in the coal business but is now unemployed. The night before last, she wanted to go to the Shaoxing Theater, but her husband stopped her, and they started arguing. Afterwards, she was so angry that she secretly took a heavy dose of crude opium and committed suicide. It was not until 2:30 AM the next morning that her husband noticed. He hired a car and sent her to Renji Hospital for treatment, but it was ineffective. She died at around 6:00 AM at dawn. The hospital reported it to the Songshan Road Police Station by telegram. Detective No. 169 was instructed to investigate, and a hearse was used to transport the body to the Tongren Fuyuan Hall for examination.

Tangshan Alumni Association Welcomes Old Classmates of Shanhaiguan Railway Official School 148

The current Tangshan College of Engineering of Jiaotong University originally evolved from the Shanhaiguan Railway Official School. The Shanhaiguan Official School was founded in the 22nd year of Guangxu in the Qing Dynasty and produced many engineering talents. During the Boxer Rebellion, the school building was destroyed and the school was closed. Later, Mr. Gu Liffei, a British engineer who was in charge of the school, used his accumulated funds to establish the Tangshan Mining School, which was passed down and continued in the same scale. It is actually two in one. After the establishment of the Tangshan Railway and Mining School, the name was changed several times, and it is now named Tangshan College of Engineering of Jiaotong University. Since the founding of the Republic of China, many graduates have been well-known at home and abroad in the engineering field for a long time. In particular, the graduates of the Shanhaiguan Railway School have made pioneering contributions in the railway and other engineering fields in our country, and their reputation is outstanding. They originally belonged to the same origin. The alumni associations in Tianjin and Wuhan have already been in contact with each other, regardless of each other. Yesterday, the Shanghai branch of the Tangshan Alumni Association gathered again at the Dachunghua Restaurant on Sichuan Road to welcome the old classmates of Shanhaiguan who came to Shanghai and join the association. Dozens of people arrived at one time. The Shanhaiguan classmates included Zhang Xiaoji, Qiu Liangcai, Zhang Tingrong, Xu Wenhui, Zhou Lin, and Jiang Guanying. Zhang Xiaoji, Qiu Liangcai, and Tangshan classmates Shi Jiagan and Jiang Shaoying all gave speeches and were very happy. It was decided on the spot to move the Tangshan Shanyou Association to the Chinese Engineers Association on the upper floor of the Continental Mall on Nanjing Road, and entrust Zhang Xiaoji to contact them. After the location is determined, a notice will be published in newspapers to inform the Shanhaiguan and Tangshan classmates at home and abroad and the branch offices of the alumni associations in various places to announce the original committee and solicit unanimous cooperation.

According to people in the tire industry, these latest airplane tires were originally designed to meet the need for airplanes to land anywhere. Because their air capacity is two or three times larger than ordinary air tires, they can be driven at a low pressure of sixteen pounds. Therefore, when they are retrofitted onto cars, there is a guarantee that there will be no bumps, vibrations, or tilting when turning. Also, because they have adhesive friction in all driving conditions, and because the tread area in contact with the road surface is particularly large, especially as a tire surface suitable for all seasons, they are safe and reliable, truly unparalleled.

Quarterly Preparation Report of the Four Banks Joint Treasury 155

198th Time

The Four Banks Joint Treasury is jointly established by the Yien Yieh, Kincheng, China & South Sea and the Continental Banks, specializing in the issuance of banknotes of the China & South Sea Bank. In accordance with the issuance regulations of the Treasury, banknotes are issued with full preparation. Cash preparation is at least 60%, and security preparation is at most 40%. A public announcement is made once a week, and is audited by the auditors and accountants of the Four Banks. The following is a transcript of the 198th public announcement of the Shanghai Preparation Treasury on October 14, 1933. Banknotes in circulation: 24,468,237 yuan. Total reserve: 24,468,237 yuan, including cash reserve of 19,811,137 yuan, and security reserve of 4,657,700 yuan.

The Xujiahui Observatory forecast at 4:30 pm yesterday: the sky here is overcast and foggy. The hurricane is moving slowly towards the northwest, almost stalled, and tends to turn north or northeast. There are tight northwesterly to northeasterly winds on the East China Sea. The weather is bad around Miyako Island and Okinawa. The center of the hurricane was within 60 miles of the intersection of 23 degrees north latitude and 126 degrees east longitude at 6:00 pm. The winds are fierce.
