Special Edition of Shenbao on the National Games

National Games, Day Nine: Shanghai's Iron Army Steadily Wins Men's and Women's Overall Championships 158

▲Shanghai Wins Men's Volleyball and Women's Basketball Championships, Guangdong Wins Women's Softball Championship

▲Men's Swimming Finals Set Four More National Records

Today's Finals: Soccer, Baseball, Men's and Women's Tennis, Men's Basketball, Women's Volleyball

(Nanjing, 18th) The results of the ninth day of the National Games have completely revealed the situation: the men's and women's overall championships have been won by Shanghai's Iron Army. Today saw the finals of six events: soccer, baseball, men's and women's tennis, men's basketball, and women's volleyball. Four more national records were set in swimming today. The Games will conclude on the 19th, and the closing and awards ceremony will be held at 10:00 am on the 20th.

Shanghai Wins Men's Overall Championship 159

There are a total of ten men's championships. As of yesterday, Shanghai had already won the track and field, all-around, and volleyball championships. Although the other six championships—soccer, basketball, tennis, baseball, swimming, and martial arts—will only be decided today, soccer is being contested by Shanghai and Guangdong, basketball by Shanghai and Hebei, and tennis by Shanghai and Sichuan. Shanghai has a great chance in all of them. Even if there are changes and Hebei and Sichuan each win one championship, if both the baseball championship, being contested by Ping and Guangdong, and the swimming championship, being contested by Hong Kong and Guangdong, are won by Guangdong, then Guangdong will only have three championships, while Shanghai already has four. Moreover, Guangdong did not participate in martial arts. Therefore, the men's overall championship was already won by Shanghai yesterday.

Shanghai Also Wins Women's Overall Championship 160

As for the women's events, there are a total of seven championships. Shanghai has already won the track and field and basketball championships. In today's volleyball championship, being contested by Shanghai and Beiping, Shanghai has a very high chance. Even if there is a problem and Beiping wins, and if Sichuan and Shanxi each win the tennis championship, Ping, Sichuan and Shanxi will only win one championship each, which has nothing to do with Shanghai. Although Guangdong has already won the softball championship yesterday, Guangdong has no hope in the swimming championship, which will definitely be won by Hong Kong. Guangdong did not participate in martial arts. Therefore, Shanghai has also won the women's overall championship.

Men's Volleyball

Shanghai Wins Men's Volleyball Championship: Straight Sets Victory Over Guangdong, South China Volleyball Loses to Shanghai for the First Time in History 161

(Nanjing, 18th) In the men's volleyball final, Shanghai defeated Guangdong. Thousands of spectators gathered at the venue. Guangdong's strength was not great. In yesterday's semi-final, Shanghai defeated Hong Kong, which was very tense. In the final, Shanghai did not have any special performance, but defeated Guangdong in straight sets to win the championship. The scores were 21-19, 21-15, and 21-18. This is the first time in history that South China has lost to Shanghai.

Spectators Gather Under Renowned Names 162

According to the championship rules, the game was scheduled to start at 3:00 pm. The venue only had one stand, with very few seats. The fans in Nanjing, because of the average strength of the two teams and the fact that this was the final game, expected one of the most exciting volleyball games. Therefore, the seats were already full before 2:00 pm, and both stands were packed by around 3:00 pm. The surrounding high ground was also crowded with people. The number of people was probably over five or six thousand. The Boy Scouts were very busy maintaining order, and the spectators were also very busy watching the ball go east and west.

Unstoppable Momentum and Expedited Progress 163

The Shanghai team has many veterans from the Far East Games, and their coordination is seamless. Li Lianying and Ma Yuanchen of the Guangdong team are also famous players who have fought on the battlefield for a long time. At the start of the game, the scores were very close. In the first game, Shanghai only won by one point. Afterwards, the three players in the front row tried their best to block the net, creating a situation where one person guarded the pass and was unstoppable. The score gradually surpassed the others. Guangdong was unable to catch up and lost the first game with a score of 19-21.

Deceptive Moves and Clever Seizing 164

In the second game, Guangdong served, and the momentum was average. At 3-3, the Shanghai front row saw that the opponent was frequently applying pressure, so they abandoned pressing the ball and focused on closing the door. However, they successively touched the net and were penalized five points in a row, making the score 3-8. The situation was precarious, and Guangdong had a great chance to turn the tables. Fortunately, Qiu Guangxie came in dangerously and saved the situation single-handedly, opening a bloody path. At 10-10, Guangdong's ball was sent to the front row by the middle row. Zhang Qun first saw the ball accurately, and pressed it lightly. Due to a difference of several points, the ball leaked into the zone and was self-destructive. At the change of sides, Guangdong took a one-point lead. Seeing that the opponent was very stubborn, and that Qiu Guangxie's big knife team had almost no way to use its methods, Shanghai suddenly adopted a clever attack. At the 12-12 tie, Xu Heng held the incoming ball, and Wang Jiajun moved his hand to the east, while pressing the ball to the west. Guangdong could not prevent it and lost the fortress. This scene was the most exciting. From then on, Shanghai's momentum was revived and it won the second game 21-15.

Warriors Gain Fame in the Line of Fire 165

After the second game, both sides rested briefly to prepare for the third game, in which they would open fire. The leaders of both sides convened a military meeting to discuss strategies. Guangdong also added new force, Liu Zemin, to replace Xiao Dianlian. With three axes on the court, Shanghai could not resist. In addition, the sun was so strong that it was difficult to see.

Soccer Championship: Shanghai and Guangdong Competing, To be Resolved Today

Shanghai Actually Defeated Guangdong 179

▲ Result: Straight Set Victory of Three

In the women's volleyball semi-final, Shanghai vs. Guangdong was quite tense. As a result, Shanghai won three to zero. The scores were 23-21, 21-18, 21-13. The final will be held on the 19th, with a bright future.

▲ Shanghai Ladies Worked Hard

Around 9 o'clock, referee Gao Xiwei was on the scene. Both Shanghai and Guangdong had supporters cheering from behind the scenes, with powerful and radiant momentum, each with great ambition. Shanghai ladies went south, Xiao Jieying sent out troops and lost generals, gaining nothing. The daughters of Southern Yue rose up and claimed supremacy, scoring four consecutive points. Shanghai worked hard, and seeing Xiao Zhijie coordinating back and forth, she succeeded immediately, creating a 4-4 tie. But just as the waves were calming, a hurricane arose again. Guangdong quickly pursued and scored three more points. Shanghai's Qian Shuyi did not flinch. Seeing the approaching ball, she jumped high over the net, and the ball died in the Guangdong zone. From then on, Shanghai had smooth sailing, ending the first half with 11 to 10. In the second half, Guangdong rose up again to meet the challenge, but their skills in saving险 were no match. The ball landed in an area where no one was guarding, and Hong Kong went all out to save it but failed. In the second ball, the Shanghai team's front row blocked the ball very well, winning first with 23 to 21.

▲ Daughters of Southern Yue Succumb

The generals of Guangdong are good at attacking, but one small mistake will negate the entire plan. The second set also started strongly, once creating a 6 to 1 lead with a very clever killing technique. But there were people rushing in front, while the back was empty. At 9 to 8, Shanghai scored three consecutive points. In the next set, both sides had no amazing performances. Shanghai, relying on an empty fort strategy, defeated Guangdong again with 21 to 18. In the third set, Shanghai's Li Po was tired and could not enter the game. She was replaced by Miss Wang Xuehua. The new force was outstanding, seizing key positions. At that time, Shanghai's momentum was rampant, and the second and third rows made many saves. Although the Guangdong ladies combined offense and defense, it was still difficult to turn the tide. They were defeated 11 to 8. In the next round, Guangdong did not slack off due to the loss. General Situ Wei was even more active. The Shanghai ladies were repeatedly surrounded, but fortunately, the back was reliable, and they saved the ball. However, their cherry lips were smeared with rouge, and their bodies were half-covered in hot sweat. The Shanghai ladies then won with a fierce attack and cheering, defeating the famous Guangdong team three straight. The tables have turned. In the championship match between Shanghai and Beiping on the 19th, we will see the spoiled and pampered ladies of the Shanghai team roar like the lioness of Hedong.

Guangdong Defeated Shanghai to Win the Championship ▲ Result: Eleven to Ten ▲ Shanghai Had a Great Advantage with Ten to Five in the First Five Innings ▲ Shanghai Pitcher Zou Shande Had Excellent Skills ▲ The Guangdong Team Was Good at Hitting and Won the Final Victory 182

(Nanjing, 18th Dispatch) The Shanghai-Guangdong women's softball final was held at 9:00 AM on the 18th. Shanghai's momentum was strong, and they had an advantage of ten to five in the first five innings. In the sixth inning, Guangdong broke the cauldron and tried to retaliate, hitting many safe hits. The Shanghai team's lineup was greatly panicked, and Guangdong scored six points in a row. As a result, Shanghai suffered a miserable defeat with ten to eleven. The championship fell into the hands of Guangdong.

▲ Pitching Technique

Regarding pitching technique, the Shanghai pitcher was Zou Shande, a high jump athlete, and her pitching skills were excellent. She killed two of three batters in a row when she went on the field, leaving Guangdong with no chance to develop. In the third inning, she killed one of three batters. Unexpectedly, in the sixth inning, her arm strength declined, and the balls she threw were weak. She was repeatedly hit by the opponent and suffered a miserable defeat by one point, which was a pity. As for the Guangdong pitchers, Zhong Shuqing in the first four innings and Ruan Rou in the last two innings, their skills were average. Shanghai's catcher Tang Yueying was not as stable as Guangdong's Zeng Shuyi. In terms of team lineup and arrangement, Shanghai seemed to be better, but their batting ability was not as good as the Guangdong team. Apart from Zeng Huiqiong, the outfielders in Shanghai were generally not confident. Half of Shanghai's large score loss in the sixth inning was due to the mistake of left fielder Xu Wenying, and there were also many errors on Shanghai's third base, which was the reason for the defeat.

▲ Taking the Initiative

Shanghai attacked first. At the beginning, Sun Zheng went on stage and got on base, followed by Li Baohui. Lu Puzhen and Meng Jian hit long balls, and Sun and Li survived. Guangdong made frequent mistakes and was embarrassed by ground balls. Meng, Zeng, and Tang took advantage of the opponent's mistakes and returned to base one after another, scoring five points in a row. When Guangdong went on stage, Zou Shande killed two of three batters in a row, killing two people. Mao Shaofang's high ball went off the field, and they were at a loss. Guangdong scored two points. Shanghai's Xu Wenying went on stage and sneaked to the base. Xiang Shaofen sent Xu back to base, scoring one point. Faced with this setback, they carefully guarded. Guangdong's third baseman Liang Shiyi caught Lu Puzhen's high ball and sent it to first base again, performing a double play. After switching sides, Guangdong's Wu Peiqi went down, and Huang Hanxian and Liang Shiyi hit safe hits in a row. Chen continued to return to base, scoring two points. The score in this inning was one to two. In total, Shanghai six, Guangdong two.

▲ Extreme Advantage

After Shanghai's Meng Jian's high ball was killed, Zeng Huiqiong hit a long ball. The left field made a mistake, and she safely landed on base. Pan Yueying sent Xu back to base, and Ren Shu and Zou Shande each hit a safe hit. Dang Ren also scored two points. Guangdong's Li Yu got a safe hit but went off the field without success. Shanghai then had an extreme advantage of nine to two. The championship seemed to be in the bag. Under the great defeat, Guangdong tried to cheer up, and their momentum gradually improved. In the fourth inning, the first three people in a row went down and failed to occupy base. Guangdong's Mao Shaofang went on stage, and her high ball was caught and died. Wu Peiqi hit a long ball and shot to the right. Zeng Huizhen missed, and the ball flew far out of the field. Wu safely returned to base. Huang Hanxian hit a safe hit, Liang Shiyi's high ball went off the field, and Zeng Shuyi also hit a home run, adding two more points. However, Shanghai still won with nine to five.

▲ Failure to Reach the Goal

In the fifth inning, Shanghai's Zeng, Pan, and Ren all went down with empty balls, and Guangdong's catching was very commendable. Guangdong also went down with three people in a row, with no progress. In the sixth inning, Shanghai's Xu Fuying hit a safe hit, and Sun Jing sent Xu back to base, scoring only one point. Guangdong's Mao Bingfang went on stage and was killed in three strikes, but the formation suddenly became chaotic afterwards. Zou Shande's arm strength declined, and Guangdong's momentum was greatly enhanced, scoring four points in a row. After Chen Jiaai's high ball went down, Lin Jie had already hit two empty balls, thinking there was hope of going down, but Shanghai lost again and again and lost two more points. At this time, Guangdong had already won with eleven to ten. After Ma Xingyan landed on base, Zhong Shuqing sent her back to base, but Zhong's foot stepped out of the line while hitting the ball, and the referee judged her foul and out of the game. Guangdong insisted that it was not allowed, and a dispute arose, and the game was stopped for about a quarter of an hour. After the base referee Wu Bangwei explained with all his strength, it was decided that Guangdong would be off the field, and Ma's one point would not count. In the seventh inning, Shanghai's counterattack was ineffective and they failed to reach their goal. Guangdong then won the championship. The ball referee was Hou Luoxun.

In the second match of the men's basketball semi-finals, Hebei faced Nanjing. Although Nanjing had defeated the Philippine Overseas Chinese team, they were ultimately no match for Hebei. Both sides of the court were completely dominated by Hebei.

▲Hebei Dominates Throughout Zhao Shouchang scored one point on a free throw due to a foul by Wei Haiqing. Tang Baokun and Shen Yugong each scored with a layup. Xian Zhuanghuai responded in kind. After that, Hebei dominated throughout. Tang Baokun occasionally made steals, and Shen Yugong's shooting accuracy was exceptional. In an instant, Hebei had already scored twenty-two points. Nanjing called another timeout. Li Gongyu felt inspired by Zhuanghuai and made two shots. At halftime, Hebei led 32-12 over Nanjing.

▲Nanjing Constantly Submissive In the second half, Hebei made numerous substitutions. Little Liu's technique was not inferior to Little Tang's, and Lian Su's skill was not diminished. Nanjing could only try to create difficulties. Liu Mengji made several long throws, but they still could not penetrate under the basket. Zhao Shouchang and Zhang Jingbao's interception skills were a cut above the rest. Shen Yugong's active running made him a talent to watch. Ma Qingzong's shooting for Nanjing was also commendable, scoring three baskets. Wei Haiqing, an old general, also made contributions, but they were ultimately no match for the divine prowess of the Hebei team. In the end, Hebei won 57-28, securing a spot in the finals.

Zhang Boling Discusses the Need for a Large-Scale Physical Education Movement, Next All-China Games Still in Beijing in 1935, Preparations for Participation in the Far Eastern Games Have Begun 198

(Nanjing, 18th) Chief Referee Zhang Boling told reporters on the 18th that many records have been broken at this All-China Games, proving that China's physical education has made significant progress. In particular, the athletes and officials have been able to abide by the rules and regulations without disputes, and the spirit of emphasizing sportsmanship is deeply admirable. However, there are still unfinished matches, such as the Shanghai-Liaoning soccer match and the Guangdong-Shanghai men's basketball match. This is the most undesirable thing about the Games. Athletes must endure any difficulties and fight to the end, which is the spirit they should have. Unexpectedly, after the Liaoning-Shanghai soccer dispute the other day, the Guangdong-Shanghai basketball match today ended on bad terms again. According to the referees' reports, both disputes were caused by intense competition during the matches, with the two teams arguing with each other, which is normal. However, spectators and athletes impersonating spectators made noises and shouted "fight," disturbing the athletes' spirit and disrupting the competition, resulting in the matches not being able to finish.

Large-Scale Physical Education Movement 199

This proves that the Chinese public does not yet understand the nature of competition and has a childish understanding of sports. Therefore, I strongly advocated at the banquet of President Wang yesterday that China should have a large-scale physical education movement to allow the general public to deeply understand the importance and nature of sports and then develop an interest in sports. If we continue to work hard from now on, the health of the Chinese nation will definitely make considerable progress in ten years. Currently, the government is using political power through the Physical Education Committee of the Ministry of Education to order provincial and municipal governments to promote physical education. On the civilian side, there are also organizations such as the National Physical Education Association and regional physical education associations. With both sides working together, future progress can be expected.

The Fierce and Brave Guangdong Women's Basketball Team (Wang Kai)

Next All-China Games 200

The next All-China Games will still be held at the Central Stadium in 1935, which can be held every four years, alternating with the Far Eastern Games. Regional sports meets, such as those in North China, should be held once a year. Only after the provinces and cities have built complete and grand stadiums will they be qualified to invite the Games to be held in their province or city. If we promote this year by year, in a few years, all provinces and cities will have complete sports facilities. Next year's North China Games will be held in Tianjin. Tianjin is urgently proceeding with the proposal of a sports stadium. It is hoped that Central China, East China, and other regions will follow the North China method and gradually expand sports facilities year by year.

Next Year's Far Eastern Games 201

As for the preparations for the National Physical Education Association to participate in next year's Far Eastern Games,

it has been decided that the Standing Committee of the Association will form a separate committee to oversee everything. Regarding the selection of Chinese athletes to attend, the committee will collect opinions from all parties and carefully select them. The Association's regular expenses are very small. In addition to the annual payment of 25 yuan per unit, it is planned to contact the Ministry of Education to ask for a considerable subsidy. However, the Association's temporary expenses are quite large, such as all the expenses for attending the Far Eastern Games next year and the World Games in 1936. Currently, we are finding ways to raise funds.

Quick Notes on Men's and Women's Swimming 203

▲Men's 1500m Freestyle Final (Nanjing, 18th) There were a total of seven participants in the 1500m final. Surprisingly, as many as three withdrew mid-race. As a result, only four people completed the entire distance. Shi Xingteng took the lead from the start and maintained the lead throughout, swimming tirelessly. He also possessed the prowess of his older brother, Xinglong, who won the one-mile freestyle title at the previous Hangzhou All-China Games. By the 750-meter mark, he had already surpassed the second-place swimmer by about 50 meters. Having completed the entire distance, he won by a margin of 160 meters over the second-place swimmer. The second-place swimmer, Guo Zhenheng, used the "W" style for one-third of the race. The future of the third-place swimmer, Shi Xinglong, is also very promising. The champion, Shi Xingteng's time of 23 minutes 27 seconds, broke the national record.

▲Men's 400m Freestyle Final There were six participants. At the start, Chen Qisong from Guangdong and Shi Xingteng from Liaoning were neck and neck. But by the 200-meter mark, Shi had distanced himself from Chen by 30 meters. Chen seemed to be running out of steam and was overtaken by Wang Honglong from Fujian. Before long, Shi Shupe i from Guangdong also surpassed Chen by about one meter. Shi led all the way, finishing about 40 meters ahead of second-place Wang Honglong. Second place beat third place by about 5 meters, and third place beat fourth place by about 3 meters. Shi's time was 5 minutes 51.9 seconds, breaking Huang Maoyuan's national record of 6 minutes 8.8 seconds.

▲Women's 100m Freestyle Preliminary The event was divided into two groups, with only four participants in each group. The top three from each group qualified. In the first group, Chen Huanqiong of Guangdong took first place, Yang Xiuqiong of Hong Kong took second, and He Wenya of Qingdao took third. When the second group started, the entire audience applauded like thunder, eager to see the Oriental standard beauty, Yang Xiuqiong, take the field. Yang did not disappoint and secured the title of the second group. Shi Xinglong's younger sister, Shi Ruisheng, was selected in the first group. She is young and weak, but her achievement is remarkable.

President Wang Addressed All Athletes Yesterday 206

(Nanjing, 18th) President Wang hosted a banquet for all athletes and officials of the All-China Games at 8:00 PM on the 18th and personally received them.

Nanjing, 18th, President of the Executive Yuan Wang Jingwei addressed all the athletes at the basketball court on the evening of the 18th. Ladies and gentlemen of the All-China Games Organizing Committee, athletes, the All-China Games has achieved unprecedented success since its opening on National Day, thanks to the tireless efforts of all of you. This is not only a source of immense gratitude and consolation for those of you who have participated, but also a source of joy and excitement for people all over the country when they hear this news. What the All-China Games has demonstrated is, first, progress, and second, widespread participation. The efforts of the athletes have resulted in performances that are close to the Far Eastern records and have broken national records. This proves that no matter what, as long as we work hard, we can make progress. If we continue to work hard from now on, then breaking the Far Eastern and world records in the next All-China Games will not be impossible. This kind of effort and proof of progress gives us immense gratitude and consolation. The enthusiastic participation of the masses in this All-China Games, and the large number of spectators, is an unexpected honor for everyone. This undoubtedly gives a profound impression to the general public, stimulating a strong interest and enthusiasm for sports. We can believe that after this Games, the development of sports will be more widespread among the national population. This is another thing that gives us immense gratitude and consolation. The expressions of this All-China Games are one of progress and one of widespread participation. What I sincerely pray for you is that you will continue to seek progress and continue to seek widespread participation. Every athlete should strive for progress at all times, encouraging each other to seek progress, and should also at all times set an example, guiding the national population to work together for progress. To transform weakness into strength depends on this. The meaning of sports is not limited to physical training but also lies in mental training. Every athlete, in terms of private morality, should pay attention to physical and mental cleanliness, and all bad habits should be eliminated. Otherwise, the qualification of an athlete cannot be maintained for long. In terms of public morality, all actions should be collectivized and disciplined. Otherwise, being disorganized and chaotic will inevitably lead to bravery in private matters and cowardice in public battles. The above are all basic conditions for refining the spirit. As for physical training, striving to be at the end of the Shanghai baseball team.

Mrs. Maddy Claims to Return to the World Stage 211

▲ Will Participate in Championships Again Next Year

(Reuters, San Francisco, 17th) World tennis queen Mrs. Maddy declared today that she has decided to return to the world tennis stage. The lady said, "I will strive to win by competing in tennis championships." Regarding her physical health, the lady said that she has gradually recovered and can walk as usual, but it will still take time to return to her former championship form. She has decided to participate in competitions again next year and will start by practicing swimming, which is currently her only form of exercise because swimming does not strain her legs, as her legs cannot bear to stand for extended periods anymore.

At the same time, the lady denied any contact regarding becoming a professional tennis player, but she has rejected a film request, saying that she is very satisfied with her life these past months and does not need it.

The lady withdrew from the final of the Linshan All-American Women's Tennis Tournament this year against Miss Jie Gubai, which caused a lot of speculation. However, it has now been confirmed that it was due to her physical inability to continue the competition.

Wonderful Tennis Performance: Lin Baohua Unexpectedly Overwhelms Xu Chengji 213

▲ Result: 3-1 Victory

Lin Baohua: : : Superb skills, a lifetime masterpiece

Xu Chengji: : : Exhausted and unable to fulfill his wishes

(Nanjing, 18th) There were no men's or women's tennis matches on the 18th. There were few people on the tennis court, but a wonderful performance began in this quiet atmosphere. Therefore, at the beginning of the battle, there were only a few spectators, only a hundred or so people. After two sets were over, the news spread like wildfire, and the audience flocked in, filling every seat, no less than the Xu-Qiu battle on the 17th morning. People were surprised to learn that Lin had won two sets in a row, and some even disbelieved it.

The Cause and Effect of Victory and Defeat 214

Objectively speaking, Lin's performance that day was particularly good. His serve was as heavy as a cannonball, his shots were as fast as arrows leaving the bow, and his volleys were unpredictable, all of which could defeat the enemy. Moreover, he was quick in running and effective in saving the ball, and his mistakes were extremely rare. This was the reason for Lin's victory and Lin's masterpiece in his life. Xu, on the other hand, was somewhat arrogant and careless because he had defeated Qiu Feihai in the morning of the 17th. This was the biggest reason for his failure in this match. As a result, his performance was greatly reduced, and he was completely different from Xu Chengji on the 17th morning.

Showing Supernatural Power and Winning Two Sets in a Row 215

At the beginning of the first set, Lin gathered his courage and attacked vigorously, while Xu found it difficult to parry and eventually suffered defeat. Lin then won the first set with a score of 6-1. In the second set, Lin took advantage of his victory and won four games in a row, while Xu was at a loss and only won the fifth and seventh games. As a result, Lin won again with a score of 6-2.

Displaying Heroism and Gaining Momentum in Resistance 216

However, Xu was by no means weak. After losing two sets, he had to be careful and cautious. From the third set onwards, Xu launched attacks and returned the favor, also winning four games in a row, while Lin only won the fifth and seventh games, just like the previous set. Xu pulled back one set with a score of 6-2.

Trying to Save the Situation but Unable to Do So 217

The fourth set was the key to victory or defeat, but Xu's serve in the first game was immediately taken advantage of. Although he tried his best to resist afterwards, he was rarely effective. He wanted to save the situation, but things did not go as he wished. Moreover, because he was too eager to win, he made frequent mistakes. In the end, Lin won the fourth set again with a score of 6-4. In total, Lin won with a score of 3-1.

Furthermore, after this reorganization, the school issues as many as sixteen types of lecture notes, and even the elective courses are issued up to six types. As for the homework, they are all personally marked by the original professors of the lecture notes. A monthly exam is held once a month in accordance with the regulations to arouse students' interest in research. The lecture notes are sent out four times a month, that is, once a week, with about 100,000 words each time, and it is planned to send them continuously without interruption. Therefore, students can obtain more than one million words of lecture notes at the end of the year. In addition to studying during the study period, students can also use these volumes for permanent reference. The school's continued recruitment of the third session of new students will close soon. Those who are interested in journalism can quickly register for admission, and those who have already received the test questions should submit them as soon as possible to complete the admission procedures and achieve their study goals as soon as possible.

Shenbao National Goods Weekly

National Goods Forum

Who is Willing to Be an Enemy of National Goods? 222

—Yang 𦰃

Nowadays, most modern women and fashionable students only favor foreign goods in terms of clothing, food, housing, and transportation. Some say that if this continues, these women will be no less than enemies of national goods. How painful is this statement! Chinese women are all citizens of the Republic of China and receive corresponding education. Who does not love their country? Everyone already knows that the country should be loved, and people should know to use and believe in national goods. Who is willing to be an enemy of national goods? The reason why national goods are not universally enjoyed by the Chinese people should be attributed to both sides:

First, from the consumer's perspective:

(1) Break the Vanity: Most men and women who grew up in Shanghai are influenced and cultivated by the novelty of imported goods, believing that the most elegant and luxurious thing to use is imported goods, so much so that they cannot boast to relatives and neighbors without it. This is completely poisoned by vanity. In fact, the most glorious and honorable thing is to use domestically produced goods. The British queen wears Lancashire cotton cloth, and the whole country follows suit, with everyone taking pride in wearing domestic cloth, which is one proof. If everyone can shift this concept and consider using foreign goods to be shameful and using domestic products to be honorable, then the promotion of national goods will be quick to influence.

(2) Should Have a Sacrificial Heart: National goods are still in their infancy today, which cannot be denied. Those who use national goods, if they feel that the quality of national goods is not perfect, may as well improve it gradually. If the price of national goods is high, they may as well sacrifice temporarily. It must be known that the quality of national goods today is different from what it was five years ago, and even more different from what it was ten years ago. If everyone can have the determination to sacrifice and help together, there will be no limit to future progress.

(3) Should Have a Guiding Heart: Why should national goods be promoted? Because national goods still need to be improved. Therefore, when we use national goods, if we feel that there is something unsatisfactory, we should not have a disgusted heart, but a guiding heart. Where should we imitate, where should we improve, which points should be promoted, which points should be reformed, so that things will improve day by day, and the products will have the hope of being refined. In Japan, a public association must stipulate an improvement fee in a certain industry, which is used to reward the industry for improving products or for testing purposes. If our people can have this ambition, whenever they go to a national goods company or a factory to purchase supplies, if they feel that there is something that should be improved, they may as well propose it on the spot and provide guidance in many ways. I know that national goods manufacturers are fighting for national goods, and they will naturally be happy to adopt it.

Second, from the producer's perspective:

(1) Eliminate Taking Advantage of the Opportunity to Get Rich: Not only modern women and fashionable students are the enemies of national goods, but also national goods merchants who take advantage of the opportunity to get rich. There are often some unpatriotic merchants who take advantage of the popularity of national goods to raise prices and seek only profit, which discourages those who are enthusiastic about using national goods. This is no less than destroying national goods. The national goods industry must not have this mentality.

(2) Do Not Produce Poorly: The credibility of national goods lies entirely in the quality and durability of the products. If you have a fluke mind, produce poorly, and seek temporary gain, and consider deceiving people as a good plan, this suicide policy should be eliminated immediately.

(3) Do Not Disguise: There are many opportunities to make money in society. Why bother to violate your conscience and engage in this unspeakable trick. Obviously, it is a Japanese product, but the trademark is changed to falsely claim that it is a domestic product. Obviously, it is an imported product, but it is secretly disguised and falsely claimed to be self-made. As a result, even those who love to use national goods are fooled and become suspicious, losing their belief in loving national goods. This is just enough to create opportunities for dumping foreign goods. This is no less than an enemy of national goods, and their crimes cannot be enumerated.

Who is willing to be an enemy of national goods? It is hoped that both production and sales will work together to establish a new life for the future of national goods.

Please Teachers to Take Responsibility for Promoting National Goods 223

— Yu Youqing

We transfer the words "Ten Years of Lessons" said by King Goujian of Yue to teachers all over the country. I feel most painful about one thing, which is that many young men and women have become loyal comrades in promoting imported goods. My friend, who is in charge of a school in a certain place, often tells me that middle school students and college students in recent years are very enthusiastic about national affairs. However, on the contrary, they all use foreign goods as their daily needs. Almost one day cannot be without foreign goods to decorate their bodies. Especially those women who shout slogans, from head to toe, all succumb to the power of foreign goods. Therefore, many people with a calm attitude often laugh at young men and women for having contradictory toys. But then again, this is not the sin of young men and women. It is the teachers who guide the youth and take responsibility for education who cannot escape the blame. Because young people are influenced and assimilated by society, they tend to like foreign goods. Being a teacher is not just responsible for teaching, and other things can be ignored. Of course, in addition to teaching, all the morbid weaknesses of young people should be corrected and guided. Whether in the classroom or after class, use sincere words and attitudes to make students who value foreign goods suddenly change their personality and become a young person who uses national goods. I think this effect is greater than any responsibility. The impact is also faster. Especially female teachers in girls' schools, take the lead in using national goods and use loyal words to persuade students who like to use foreign goods, so that her cold ashes suddenly become hot. Foreign goods lose people's purchase, and even if they are not resisted, they will disappear. Otherwise, not buying a certain product and changing to a certain product is just replacing violence with violence. What is the use? Dear teachers all over the country, do a propaganda work. If it combines the ten years of lessons of the King of Yue, and continues like this, after ten years, foreign goods will be eradicated. I can make an oath: "Whoever kills me to thank the people of the country."

"Autumn Big Bargain" and National Goods 224

— Xuan Yu

The shadow of the autumn wind, the banners of "Autumn Big Bargain" on various roads, have begun to flutter. All the dazzling advertisements have also exerted their power and touched our eyes, as if telling us that "Autumn" has arrived, because with the change of climate, people's lives will undergo a major change, and if you want to prepare early - add objects, then the major shopping malls and shops are waiting for you.

Naturally, discounts are the only tool to attract customers to buy, and at the same time, it is also the best opportunity to establish a good social reputation. At this time, our national goods factories' sales agencies, national goods companies, national goods shopping malls, and self-operated stores everywhere, in order to respond to the times, must also follow them to hold a grand discount. However, here, we must have a deep view. We must know that the so-called "discount" of general ordinary stores now is continuous and commonplace. This kind of act that only owns a false name and has no practical actions, is nothing more than using this nominal appeal to absorb general purchasing power and take advantage of the time to move. The shallowness of his views, the fragmentary nature and the inability to last, are also self-evident. Then, if we take this policy to make our national goods agency's position to be biased, it is naturally wrong, however, because our discounts must at least contain the following two important meanings:

1. Take the opportunity to gain trust in society: This can now be discussed only in the Shanghai area. There are indeed many sales agencies for national goods, but those who sell foreign goods have not disappeared. So when this discount is held at the same time, we should be how to faithfully sacrifice, and strive for genuine goods at a fair price. Be realistic, and have an amazing performance, so that all sectors of society will be more credible.

2. Take the opportunity to introduce new products: This is to take advantage of this opportunity to introduce the latest new products from various factories to the public for awareness and adoption, just like the China National Goods Company's discount this time, and try to introduce Meiya's silk crepe and butterfly wool, etc. In the large window, it is very conspicuously displayed, and his sales standard will eventually expand gradually from small to large.

In short, we must take "promotion" and "promotion" as the premise, and hold discounts with meaningful and valuable plans. If we have a long-term vision, the current sacrifice will be the future effect. The two are absolutely proportional. Try to think, assuming that every Chinese loves to use national goods and foreign goods disappear, are we still afraid that national goods have no market at that time!

National Goods Discussion

Discussion on Several Important Issues in Promoting National Goods 225

— Ziqiang

National Goods - National Goods - Calling Broken Eardrums - Dazzling Eyes - This is the New Contribution of the National Goods Year - This is the First Time in History -

We only need to pay attention to the newspaper, and we can see the news about national goods, as well as the big discounts from various companies and merchants promoting national goods - especially the National Goods Exhibition, which is opened in time, which is worth commemorating! Now, I would like to buy its one-sided foolishness to discuss several questions, which should not be closed to the door!

1. Promoting national goods should expand the scope: - Whenever major companies and major merchants have big discounts, the sacrificed goods are often limited to this city; in this way, people in this city can get the moon first near the water, and people in other cities have to drool for three feet, and want to buy but cannot, so expanding the scope is the first important issue.

2. Transactions in other cities should be given a grace period: - Other cities

It is too far from this city, or places where transportation is not available, and the good opportunity is lost. Although the postmark is used as proof, it is not a thorough

Good way, to make the benefits of this city and other cities equal, unless the time is extended, it is convenient for the slowly arrived other city

3. Mailed goods should take care of credit: - The only agency for purchasing goods in other cities is the post office for transmission. However, when buying goods in person, there is still a mixture of fakes, and mail orders are even more unimaginable. For the sake of being realistic and taking care of credit, it should be genuine goods at fair prices, without deceiving the distant and near.

The wholesale and retail prices should be uniform: - The Chinese business community has never paid attention to business ethics, selling empty and buying empty, relying on it as the only ability, and the prices are also not uniform. Unless you are a person in the know, you can buy cheap goods. The old men in the countryside will suffer, so a uniform price is also worth discussing.

The above-mentioned are the most important issues in promoting national goods, small words, which are related to the future of national goods, big words, which are related to the lifeline of the country. Now, although the rural areas have gone bankrupt, it has reached the point where the mountains and rivers are exhausted, but there are still many畸形phenomena in society: (1) no purchasing power, (2) there is purchasing power but no place to buy. The result is that the people and national goods have little to do with each other. This is not that the people in the mainland have no relationship with national goods, but it is just that they cannot get into the door.

邰 in the Public Tea Garden 226

— Shuangqiu Bo Shu

Today, the decoration in the public tea garden has been completely changed. The tables all around the walls are full of local products such as cotton cloth, cotton yarn, cocoons, and grains, all of which are packed in glass boxes. There are twice as many people, and everyone is looking at those local products one after another. "Fellow compatriots, I know you are enlightened people, and everyone has recognized the value of the local product movement, but seeing the clothes on your bodies, the cigarettes in your hands,::: I can't help but shed tears for you! Alas, because you love to use foreign goods, 400 million taels of gold are put into the pockets of foreigners. On average, each of us Chinese has to send more than one yuan to foreigners every year. Why? Do you want to learn to be beautiful? Alas, for the sake of your beauty, you have to send 400 million taels to people every year. This is so painful! Compatriots, I used to wear suits and learn to be beautiful, but five years ago, I had long deeply realized that China would soon be destroyed by foreign economic aggression, and I had to get up to wake up our drunken compatriots - look, my blue cloth shirt, isn't it considered clothes? Must you wear a suit and foreign fabrics to be considered beautiful? To be fashionable? Alas, fellow compatriots, do you still want to be beautiful? Still want to be fashionable? Which one is enlightened, quickly make an ambition to adopt local products to the death, please come up and shake hands with me now." So I followed them to the stage, and when Dr. Tai's hand touched my hand, I suddenly felt the enthusiasm of his entire local product movement impacting my body, as if giving me a very severe punishment. I couldn't help but shed tears with them.

The National Goods Cosmetics Industry in the Past Year (II) 227

(3) Cosmetics, in a broad sense, include toothpaste, tooth powder, scented soap, cologne, hair tonic, face powder, puff powder, snow powder, etc.

After September 18th, the Northeast market, which had been competing with the Japanese for many years, had no room to intervene. This is an economic loss in addition to the loss of territory.

. It is not the time for the Chinese to care about it. As for the Xiangya Company, due to unsuccessful operations, it has been reorganized repeatedly. Fortunately, it is still able to maintain. Cosmetics pay attention to decoration. The labels, paper boxes, and tin boxes used are all made domestically. The high-quality glass bottles are often taken from foreign countries. Now, almost all of them are contracted by domestic material factories. The products are no different from foreign goods. According to statistics, many rights and interests can be recovered every year. The rise of industry often has a linked effect. Industrialists should know what to learn from to enrich the people's livelihood.

Random Notes from Boshu Studio 228

— Rong Yu

Big A-Fu and Foreign Dolls

Round, powdered faces, painted with two dots of rouge; square foreheads, combed with a few strands of bangs: a constantly smiling face, resembling the Maitreya Buddha. This is the clay figure produced in Huishan, the well-known Big A-Fu.

When Big A-Fu arrived at little Ling’s home, little Ling loved it very much. She opened her small mouth to sing for it; clapped her small hands to dance for it; whatever cakes or snacks she had, she would give it to eat first; and at night, she would sleep with it. Big A-Fu also loved little Ling, facing her silently, just grinning.

A month later, Big A-Fu encountered misfortune in its fate palace. Little Ling washed its face, and the rouge and powder were gone, turning into a mud-spotted face. Little Ling accidentally dropped it, and it shattered into pieces. Little Ling cried and wailed, and her mother found a foreign doll from the West to be its companion.

The foreign doll was truly beautiful, with golden hair, an apple-like face, a delicate body, and fashionable clothes, attracting little Ling to love it even more. She sang, danced, fed it snacks, and slept with it, dedicating all the love she had for Big A-Fu to the foreign doll. "One only sees the new person smile, who hears the old person cry?" The foreign doll was smug, and Big A-Fu shed tears in the corner. One day, the foreign doll got caught in the rain and was soaked all over. Little Ling roasted it by the fire to dry its clothes and warm its body. Little Ling continued to roast it. With a "sizzle," the foreign doll turned into a fire child, and the scent of resin and rosin filled the room. Little Ling cried loudly, realizing that her two small hands had been burned into red, swollen blisters.

The foreign doll harmed little Ling, making her cry while eating and cry while sleeping. She resented it for burning her two small hands and feet, and she was sick for a month.

When little Ling recovered, Big A-Fu came again. She said, "I love you, and I hope everyone loves you. You are a symbol of harmony and won't stab people in the back. I never want to see the face of that harmful foreign doll again."

Big Pancake and Fried Dough Sticks

Waking up in the morning, I walk around the fields. The sky is clear, the earth is silent, and a fresh morning air rushes into my nostrils, refreshing my internal organs like sweet dew.

My stomach is slightly hungry, and the freshly baked pancakes and freshly fried dough sticks make my mouth water. I spent nine copper coins on two pancakes and a fried dough stick, chewing and swallowing, tasting crispy, salty, and sweet, all at once, and shouting, "Wonderful! Wonderful!"

In Shanghai, I also chew on bread every day, even cream bread made with American flour. It's neither sweet nor salty, neither sour nor savory, how can it have the human touch of big pancakes and fried dough sticks? Those who like it sweet add jam; those who like it salty spread it with white lard or sandwich it with ham slices. The taste is still better, but one meal of bread is already worth the price of a feast.

Big pancakes and fried dough sticks seem to be exclusive to the proletariat; the rich disdain to bite into them. In fact, they are rich in nutrients, surpassing bird's nest and white fungus. —Whether bird's nest and white fungus are nourishing is still a question in new medicine.—Those who are used to eating bird's nest and white fungus certainly won't chew on big pancakes and fried dough sticks; those who are used to biting on Western bread also won't chew on big pancakes and fried dough sticks, so big pancakes and fried dough sticks are also carrying out their civilian work.

But I still like them after all, and I also advise people to bite into them. At this moment, a gust of wind brings a burst of singing. I wonder if it's students singing or workers singing? The lyrics go:

"Big pancakes and fried dough sticks, big pancakes and fried dough sticks, crispy fried dough twists, three copper coins for one, so delicious! So delicious!"

China Chemical Industrial Society 22nd Anniversary Special Issue

Demands to the Government from the Perspective of Supporting National Products 229

— Li Zufan

Ever since the May Fourth Movement, the Chinese people have been alarmed by the severity of foreign economic aggression and the decline of traditional domestic handicrafts. People with lofty ideals have risen up to jointly promote national products in an active manner to save themselves. However, for more than ten years, not only has there been a lack of significant results, but also, upon inspecting the customs trade registers, imports have increased year after year! This phenomenon is partly due to the fact that the organization of our national product industry is not comprehensive enough, the steps are not consistent enough, resulting in divergent views and weak strength. However, the failure of the government to effectively implement protective policies is a major obstacle to the development of national product industries.

After the National Government established its capital in Nanjing, all policies were based on the Three Principles of the People, with the principle of promoting production and improving people's livelihood. It clearly proclaimed to our people: First, "Support agriculture and industry," and second, "Save the country through industry." These words are well said. The national product industrial and commercial circles are in an environment of groaning and suffering every day, leading the way and waiting for our government to provide relief and support. However, after four years of political tutelage, the disorder of politics remains the same, the decline of people's livelihood remains the same, so that the dumping of foreign goods and the decline of national products also remain the same. Upon investigation, the biggest reason is that the government has failed to provide the people with effective assistance. The development of a country's industry and commerce is always causally related to politics. Those European and American countries with developed industry and commerce all list the government's efforts to seek social economic stability and development as the top priority in their political program. Matters concerning supporting agriculture, industry and commerce are mostly enshrined in the constitution, special regulations are enacted, taxes are reduced and sales are promoted, and capital is used to promote their success. Everything that can benefit industry and commerce is pursued with full force. As a result, industry and commerce become more developed, the social economy becomes more prosperous, and the country's politics also become stable. On the other hand, in our country, foreign aggression and internal strife are intensifying day by day. Exorbitant taxes and levies make it difficult for people to survive. Under these circumstances, it is difficult for our national product industrial and commercial circles to seek outward development!

Recently, our government, in view of the increasingly acute world economic competition, deeply knows that without promoting national products, it is not enough to save the country from danger. It has specifically designated this year as the Year of National Products, and with political power, it has awakened the people to cooperate fully, hoping to open up a new path in this sluggish state. Observing the enthusiasm of recent exhibitions in various places, we are sincerely gratified and have more enthusiastic expectations for the promotion of national products.

However, we still have unavoidable pain that must be stated to our government. Now, please briefly state them: (1) The import tax should be urgently revised. The economic community has called for the dismantling of tariff barriers, and as a result, the barriers of various countries have been raised. Our government once revised the tax rate in May of this year; however, the tax rates on most imported goods have not been changed, so that the national products that have just sprouted are competing with the products of foreign factories with decades of large capital and low tax imports. Is the outcome still waiting to be revealed? Isn't it to maintain this status quo? I have seen that the import tax rate on raw materials for a factory is often higher than the import tax rate on finished products. This is truly contrary to encouraging industry. This is why the import tax rate must be urgently rectified.

(2) The 2.5% surtax should be abolished urgently. In addition to the 5% ad valorem tax, our country's current customs duties must also add a 2.5% surtax. The implementation of the 2.5% surtax began in 1927. The implementation of this tax was originally intended to serve as a fund for the 2.5% national treasury bonds. The initial issuance of 2.5% national treasury bonds in 1927 was 30 million yuan, and another 40 million yuan was issued in 1928. Its purpose was designated to be used for military expenditure, political expenses, and insufficient budgets, and to repay short-term loans, with the end of April 1933 as the final period for repaying principal and interest. Now that the repayment period has expired, the collection of the 2.5% surtax has no reason to exist in fact. Today, our country's industry and commerce are declining, how can we bear to pay the surtax in addition to the regular tax? If it is said that the national military and political expenses are insufficient, then since customs duties are already autonomous, the import tax should be increased to supplement them. Does our government truly intend to sympathize with the difficulties of merchants and alleviate the suffering of the people? Please start by abolishing the 2.5% surtax.

(3) All exorbitant taxes should be effectively stopped. Since the New Year's Day of 1932, our government has implemented the declaration of customs autonomy and at the same time abolished likin and all exorbitant taxes and miscellaneous levies. It has not hesitated to issue repeated orders to exempt machine-made national products from heavy levies; however, because our country's politics are not on track, warlords occupy and enrich themselves, and the central government's authority cannot reach the remote provinces. Therefore, the clear orders are equivalent to empty words, and heavy levies remain the same. For example, from Shanghai to Sichuan, Gansu, and other places, the transportation taxes and other expenses often exceed twice the value of the goods themselves. How can we seek the promotion of national products under such circumstances? If our government wants to support the development of industry and commerce, it should quickly and effectively stop this heavy levy so that national products can be sold throughout the interior; otherwise, if the promotion is biased towards the cities and foreign goods are sold in remote areas, the hope of revitalizing national products may end up being a pie in the sky.

(4) We should actively devote ourselves to transportation construction. Since the establishment of the five yuan, the facilities in all administrative aspects have gradually seen progress. Even in terms of transportation, in addition to the Ministry of Communications, a separate Ministry of Railways has been specially established to take charge of its responsibilities. Its intention to facilitate industrial and commercial transportation is undoubtedly far-reaching. However, due to incessant internal strife and foreign aggression over the years, most of the country's tax revenue has been consumed by military preparations. As a result, transportation construction has become slow. Even in the provinces of Jiangsu, Zhejiang, Anhui, and Jiangxi, which are known as the construction of Meng Jin, the various sections of the highway have been completed one after another, but their benefits only extend to travelers. As for freight transportation, it is still rarely effective. The situation in other transportation-blocked areas is even worse. If our government wants to relieve the plight of industry and commerce, it should quickly and actively rectify transportation to facilitate the transportation of the people. After all, transportation and exorbitant taxes are always in a positive ratio. If transportation can be convenient, the exorbitant taxes in the interior will lose their basis and will be easier to abolish.

The above three points are just a brief summary of the major issues that are closely related to our interests. Other issues, such as the development of industrial raw materials and the training of technical personnel, also rely on our government's practical planning to seek fundamental solutions. Now that political tutelage is about to be completed and constitutional government is about to begin, the outline for supporting agriculture, industry, and commerce has been seen in the draft constitution, and we sincerely hope that it will be passed and implemented as soon as possible.

How to Promote National Products 230

— Xing Shu

In China, a country with backward production, the production volume and consumption volume of our country's industrial products form a ratio of two to five, while at the same time, material progress is advancing by leaps and bounds. The needs of the people for industrial products can be imagined from this.

Therefore, in this Year of Promoting National Products, we want to solve the fundamental method of promoting national products. The best way is for major factories across the country to unite their operations, because the benefits of united operations are:

(1) Restricting production volume,

(2) Estimating standard prices,

(3) Concentrating talent and distributing sales,

(4) Implementing comprehensive planning,

(5) Avoiding unnecessary competition, resulting in mutual harm,

(6) Concretely seeking production and sales cooperation.

In short, our country must unite the strength of the entire industrial sector to seek a balance between production and sales volume. Mr. Fang Yexian of the China Chemical Industrial Society is actively carrying out this work, based on this purpose. For example, the launch of the China National Products Company is based on this ideal and realized. It is expected that in the near future, there will be a new development in the entire national product sector.

The Issue of Agricultural-Industrial Cooperation 231

— Mars

In modern Chinese society with backward production, I believe that the problem that needs to be solved urgently is agricultural-industrial cooperation, because in fact it has told us that the raw materials for industrial products mostly depend on the countryside, and yet in recent years our rural economy has been experiencing panic every day. Therefore, the industrial sector cannot have improved development. So from now on, if we want to increase the production volume of national products, we must cooperate with farmers in a down-to-earth manner. Now I will cite two examples below:

For example, the raw material for manufacturing insecticides is pyrethrum, but the cultivation of pyrethrum has not yet been popularized in the current domestic agriculture. Seeing that the domestic demand for insecticide raw materials is not meeting the supply every year, we have no choice but to rely on foreign pyrethrum. If we had considerable cultivation in our rural areas, then the annual harvest would be sufficient for our own use, and the agricultural-industrial problem would be adequately solved at the same time.

Another example is that the raw material for manufacturing seasonings is made from wheat beans, and the production of wheat beans requires the efforts of farmers to supply the needs of our national product factories.

China Chemical Industrial Society, on the one hand, is manufacturing new industrial products, and on the other hand, is also actively promoting agricultural products, such as promoting the planting of pyrethrum and directly signing cooperation agreements with farmers, which is a very good example. I hope that our entire agricultural sector will rise up and cooperate with us to complete that greatest wish.

The Contribution of Samsung Caramel Coloring in Industry 232

— Xin Sheng

Since the flourishing of science, the industries of various countries have had a trend of rapid progress. Various daily necessities in life, especially, are changing with each passing day. Those old industries that do not conform to scientific principles have almost all been eliminated invisibly! Our country has a vast territory and abundant resources, with a large number of factories, but unfortunately, the Chinese people only know how to stick to old methods and do not think about improvement, so it has become a country with backward production and suffers from the pain of foreign economic aggression! Generally, people with insight have long been aware of this and unanimously believe that "improving industry and increasing production" is not enough to save the country from danger! China Chemical Industrial Society was founded in the first year of the Republic, with the aim of improving industry, specializing in the use of chemical methods to manufacture various new industrial products. The products it has launched have been praised by the society. Recently, the company, in view of the unhygienic, uneconomical, and inconvenient nature of traditional sugar frying, has used chemical methods to research and manufacture "Samsung Brand New Caramel Coloring." Now, after the trial use of major soy sauce gardens, bean curd workshops, etc. across the country, they have unanimously found it satisfactory.

Samsung Brand Caramel Coloring is manufactured by chemical methods using machines. Its raw material is glucose made from wheat flour, and then the caramel coloring is made from glucose. It is steamed to extreme concentration, the material is pure, and the color is deep and clear. Compared with the old method of frying sugar, its effect has at least the following advantages:

(1) With the same effect, it can reduce costs by half, allowing manufacturers to reduce the cost of their products.

(2) The quality is pure and clean, without the drawbacks of dregs and turbidity.

(3) It is odorless, tasteless, does not ferment, and does not mold.

(4) It only needs to be dissolved in boiling water before it can be used, which is extremely convenient.

(5) The color depth has standards, and it can be used in the right amount, without the disadvantages of being too much or not enough!

(6) The quality is excellent, no less than Japanese goods, and the price is cheaper, which is enough to resist foreign goods.

In short, this new type of caramel is a new product in our country's industry. In practice, it dares to claim the four characters "high quality and low price." However, this new industrial product has not been on the market for long, and its sales have not yet become widespread. It is hoped that manufacturers in various places will adopt it for comparison and promote it unanimously, saving consumption in manufacturing, increasing cleanliness in food, and saving a part of the country's economic leakage.

Studying Artificial Beauty Methods Based on Skin Tissue 233

— Chen Huaipu

—Results Obtained from Domestic Cosmetics—

The color of the skin is due to the different amounts of pigment particles in the skin cells and within the cells, which distinguishes the various races of people. Even within the same race, people are divided into those with less pigment who have yellow skin and those with more pigment who have black skin. Therefore, we do not have to admire the beauty of the white race. Before there is a way to change the pigment, yellow people have to have yellow skin to the end, and black people have to have black skin. If we see a yellow person's skin that does not come into contact with sunlight or a patient's deathly white skin, the degree of whiteness may be more severe than that of white people's skin, but we cannot say that it is whiter than the beauty of white people. This is as ridiculous as the analogy of Madam Meng's white snow and white feathers.

When it comes to the beauty of the skin, it will never be emphasized solely on whiteness or blackness. Only when the skin is smooth and shiny can it be considered beautiful and healthy. The meaning of what we usually call skin is really very narrow. In physiology books, it is only a part of the whole skin tissue, only the outermost stratum corneum of the skin, and the several types of tissues below the stratum corneum are ignored. Even if we want the stratum corneum, which we call skin, to be smooth and shiny, we should understand the most relevant sebum.

The components of sebum under a microscope are countless small particles, a small number of glandular cells filled with fat, cell membranes that have changed, and cholesterol crystals. The chemical composition is mainly liquid lipid oil and solid soft fat, and others are composed of fat soap, a small amount of cholesterol, protein, and inorganic salts. Because this sebum contains the secretion of oil, it moisturizes the skin (stratum corneum) and makes the hair smooth: Sebum constantly performs metabolic functions, pushing the stratum corneum and dead and damaged skin tissue cells on the skin surface outward. Therefore, we find many skin flakes falling off our body, and the skin also feels oily and greasy excretions.

The reason we pay attention to skin beauty is certainly not because beauty can please people. Moreover, the amount of oxygen absorbed and the amount of carbon dioxide excreted by the human body through the skin in a day and night is almost equal to the amount inhaled and exhaled by the lungs. Naturally, we should pay attention to it. Now that we understand the general effect of skin tissue and sebum, and there is a reason why we have to pay attention to it, but human beings always want to realize the method of making the skin white and beautiful. Since the pigment cannot be transformed, they have to imagine artificial whitening methods. Many internal and external medicines that can whiten the skin have been listed, but very few can truly comfort those who crave permanent beauty methods. They have to take another step back and imagine temporary makeup methods, and then they conduct partial research from domestic cosmetic manufacturers. As a result, there are various products produced by the China Chemical Industrial Society that can be used by ladies in society every day, guaranteeing safety without side effects, and will definitely have the effect of transforming ugliness into beauty and achieving the reality of beauty.

1. Peony Scented Soap: There are many methods for distinguishing scented soap, and the best is to not contain free alkali. However, it is not suitable to contain impure saponified fat, and it is not a good product to contain many insoluble substances. Now, all kinds of soap produced by the China Chemical Industrial Society do not have this kind of problem. Especially the new product, Peony Scented Soap, is even more refined. The surface does not show white spots, which is evidence that there is no free alkali. If you cut it off and press it on white paper and look at it in the sunlight, you will not see oil stains, which is evidence that there is no impure saponified fat: If you test it under concentrated alcohol and there is no insoluble precipitate, it is evidence that it does not contain insoluble substances.

2. Fangze Cream: This is another product that is most beneficial to the skin. It is a pure fatty substance. We know that the skin can absorb all gases, but it can also absorb continuously adhering liquids and fatty substances. Therefore, this kind of fat can be absorbed and reach inside the sebum to increase its secretion function. Therefore, it is most suitable for daily application between dry and chapped skin in winter and those who lack sebum, as well as for washing the skin with pancreatic soap and after men shave.

3. Swan Powder: The easiest thing to cause skin disease in scented powder is to contain lead, even if it is a small amount, it can make the skin rough and produce many pimples after prolonged use. In severe cases, black-brown spots will appear on the skin. When lead poisoning spreads throughout the body, it can cause the body to lose weight, reduce appetite, and emit a foul odor from the mouth, because this kind of lead white powder contains non-soluble substances such as aluminum oxide and aluminum carbonate, but when it combines with sweat and fat, it becomes soluble and is very dangerous to pass through the skin and then immerse in the blood! This Swan Powder is indeed made of non-toxic magnesium carbonate and non-irritating spices, and is rich in fat, light in texture, and does not block pores.

4. Era Cream: It can not only make the skin expand and soften, resist the invasion of wind and sun, but also absorb the dirt that is prepared to be excreted in the pores, and increase the secretion function of cells, so that new cells can live in good condition, and the cells that have withered and died can be smoothly squeezed out in the metabolic state.

With these four exquisite cosmetics, used in conjunction with each other, it can be guaranteed that the skin will absolutely not be damaged, and the purpose of beauty can be achieved, so it is specially presented to the public.

Postscript to the Pyrethrum Cultivation Method 234

— Huaipu

Recently, the fourth edition of the Pyrethrum Cultivation Method, edited and written by the China Chemical Industrial Society, was written by Mr. Yu Chengru and reviewed by me. This kind of academic text does not need to be embellished. After proofreading it several times, I was fortunate enough to read the contents first and learn the planting methods, and my feelings were gathered together, and I really had to express them all.

The discovery of the function of pyrethrum was as far back as 430 years ago. After repeated dissemination, the planters are now all over the continents of Europe, Asia, and North America. The production volume should be the largest in the United States and Japan, followed by various European countries. However, when I was writing and wanting to review this book, I consulted Chinese and foreign classics extensively, but I could not find a detailed and systematic description that could be used for reference, roughly like this book. Therefore, the originality of this book is really commendable, and it is even more valuable that it is entirely based on more than ten years of planting experience and compiled, without incorporating empty theories.

The enterprise that increased its business by planting pyrethrum and adopted it as raw material in the country also started with the China Chemical Industrial Society's manufacturing of mosquito coils. I remember that since the establishment of the farm in 1917, it has accumulated more than 200 acres of land, with a perfect scale and an annual increase in production. I still remember that this year, it invited people from all walks of life who were interested in planting pyrethrum to visit the Anlangdu Experimental Farm. The scene was lively and prosperous. As a result of years of promotion, people from all walks of life have gained a deep impression.

According to the pyrethrum, the seedlings produced from seeds are better. Therefore, supplying seeds is also an urgent need. Therefore, the China Chemical Industrial Society must distribute a large amount of pyrethrum seeds to comrades every year, with the true purpose of promoting them, setting the lowest price. For example, this year's harvest of more than 80 kilograms of seeds was sold out in less than ten days, and letters ordering from various places were still coming in, so it had to purchase dozens of pounds from other farms at a high price, and at the expense of sacrifice, it still transferred them at the original price of 50 cents per market ounce, which is much different from the market price of 80 cents, more than one yuan, or even three yuan. Moreover, because the seed selection is precise, the seedlings that have been cultivated in various places have already achieved considerable results.

In recent years, the rural economy has been in crisis, and the lives of farmers have been difficult. The various crops they plant have suffered from poor harvests, and the capital invested in fertilizer, labor, and planting is difficult to recover. However, planting pyrethrum is easy and the income is even better. Usually, the net income per acre per year is 37 yuan. If you can cultivate it yourself, the income can be increased. If you carry out crop rotation, the income will be even greater. It is truly the only way to save the rural economy. It not only supplies the domestic chemical industry for production and consumption, but also recovers some vested interests!
